     436            8 : /**
     437            8 :  * Special values for `CompletionInfo['source']` used to disambiguate
     438            8 :  * completion items with the same `name`. (Each completion item must
     439            8 :  * have a unique name/source combination, because those two fields
     440            8 :  * comprise `CompletionEntryIdentifier` in `getCompletionEntryDetails`.
     441            8 :  *
     442            8 :  * When the completion item is an auto-import suggestion, the source
     443            8 :  * is the module specifier of the suggestion. To avoid collisions,
     444            8 :  * the values here should not be a module specifier we would ever
     445            8 :  * generate for an auto-import.
     446            8 :  *
     447            8 :  * @internal
     448            8 :  */
     449            8 : export enum CompletionSource {
     450            8 :     /** Completions that require `this.` insertion text */
     451            8 :     ThisProperty = "ThisProperty/",
     452            8 :     /** Auto-import that comes attached to a class member snippet */
     453            8 :     ClassMemberSnippet = "ClassMemberSnippet/",
     454            8 :     /** A type-only import that needs to be promoted in order to be used at the completion location */
     455            8 :     TypeOnlyAlias = "TypeOnlyAlias/",
     456            8 :     /** Auto-import that comes attached to an object literal method snippet */
     457            8 :     ObjectLiteralMethodSnippet = "ObjectLiteralMethodSnippet/",
     458            8 :     /** Case completions for switch statements */
     459            8 :     SwitchCases = "SwitchCases/",
     460            8 :     /** Completions for an Object literal expression */
     461            8 :     ObjectLiteralMemberWithComma = "ObjectLiteralMemberWithComma/",
     462            8 : }

     519            8 : 
     520            8 : function originIsThisType(origin: SymbolOriginInfo): boolean {
     521            8 :     return !!(origin.kind & SymbolOriginInfoKind.ThisType);
     522            8 : }
     523            8 : 
     524            8 : function originIsSymbolMember(origin: SymbolOriginInfo): boolean {
     525            8 :     return !!(origin.kind & SymbolOriginInfoKind.SymbolMember);
     526            8 : }
     527            8 : 
     528            8 : function originIsExport(origin: SymbolOriginInfo | undefined): origin is SymbolOriginInfoExport {
     529            8 :     return !!(origin && origin.kind & SymbolOriginInfoKind.Export);
     530            8 : }
     531            8 : 
     532            8 : function originIsResolvedExport(origin: SymbolOriginInfo | undefined): origin is SymbolOriginInfoResolvedExport {
     533            8 :     return !!(origin && origin.kind === SymbolOriginInfoKind.ResolvedExport);
     534            8 : }
     535            8 : 
     536            8 : function originIncludesSymbolName(origin: SymbolOriginInfo | undefined): origin is SymbolOriginInfoExport | SymbolOriginInfoResolvedExport | SymbolOriginInfoComputedPropertyName {
     537            8 :     return originIsExport(origin) || originIsResolvedExport(origin) || originIsComputedPropertyName(origin);
     538            8 : }
     539            8 : 
     540            8 : function originIsPackageJsonImport(origin: SymbolOriginInfo | undefined): origin is SymbolOriginInfoExport {
     541            8 :     return (originIsExport(origin) || originIsResolvedExport(origin)) && !!origin.isFromPackageJson;
     542            8 : }
     543            8 : 
     544            8 : function originIsPromise(origin: SymbolOriginInfo): boolean {
     545            8 :     return !!(origin.kind & SymbolOriginInfoKind.Promise);
     546            8 : }
     547            8 : 
     548            8 : function originIsNullableMember(origin: SymbolOriginInfo): boolean {
     549            8 :     return !!(origin.kind & SymbolOriginInfoKind.Nullable);
     550            8 : }
     551            8 : 
     552            8 : function originIsTypeOnlyAlias(origin: SymbolOriginInfo | undefined): origin is SymbolOriginInfoTypeOnlyImport {
     553            8 :     return !!(origin && origin.kind & SymbolOriginInfoKind.TypeOnlyAlias);
     554            8 : }
     555            8 : 
     556            8 : function originIsObjectLiteralMethod(origin: SymbolOriginInfo | undefined): origin is SymbolOriginInfoObjectLiteralMethod {
     557            8 :     return !!(origin && origin.kind & SymbolOriginInfoKind.ObjectLiteralMethod);
     558            8 : }
     559            8 : 
     560            8 : function originIsIgnore(origin: SymbolOriginInfo | undefined): boolean {
     561            8 :     return !!(origin && origin.kind & SymbolOriginInfoKind.Ignore);
     562            8 : }
     563            8 : 
     564            8 : function originIsComputedPropertyName(origin: SymbolOriginInfo | undefined): origin is SymbolOriginInfoComputedPropertyName {
     565            8 :     return !!(origin && origin.kind & SymbolOriginInfoKind.ComputedPropertyName);
     566            8 : }

     596            8 :     TypeAssertionKeywords,
     597            8 :     TypeKeywords,
     598            8 :     TypeKeyword,                    // Literally just `type`
     599            8 :     Last = TypeKeyword,
     600            8 : }
     601            8 : 
     602            8 : const enum GlobalsSearch {
     603            8 :     Continue,
     604            8 :     Success,
     605            8 :     Fail,
     606            8 : }
     607            8 : 
     608            8 : interface ModuleSpecifierResolutionContext {
     609            8 :     tryResolve: (exportInfo: readonly SymbolExportInfo[], isFromAmbientModule: boolean) => ModuleSpecifierResolutionResult;
     610            8 :     resolvedAny: () => boolean;
     611            8 :     skippedAny: () => boolean;
     612            8 :     resolvedBeyondLimit: () => boolean;
     613            8 : }
     614            8 : 
     615            8 : type ModuleSpecifierResolutionResult = "skipped" | "failed" | {
     616            8 :     exportInfo?: SymbolExportInfo | FutureSymbolExportInfo;
     617            8 :     moduleSpecifier: string;
     618            8 : };
     619            8 : 
     620            8 : function resolvingModuleSpecifiers<TReturn>(
     621            8 :     logPrefix: string,
     622            8 :     host: LanguageServiceHost,
     623            8 :     resolver: codefix.ImportSpecifierResolver,
     624            8 :     program: Program,
     625            8 :     position: number,
     626            8 :     preferences: UserPreferences,
     627            8 :     isForImportStatementCompletion: boolean,
     628            8 :     isValidTypeOnlyUseSite: boolean,
     629            8 :     cb: (context: ModuleSpecifierResolutionContext) => TReturn,
     630            8 : ): TReturn {
     631            8 :     const start = timestamp();
     632            8 :     // Under `--moduleResolution nodenext`, we have to resolve module specifiers up front, because
     633            8 :     // package.json exports can mean we *can't* resolve a module specifier (that doesn't include a
     634            8 :     // relative path into node_modules), and we want to filter those completions out entirely.
     635            8 :     // Import statement completions always need specifier resolution because the module specifier is
     636            8 :     // part of their `insertText`, not the `codeActions` creating edits away from the cursor.
     637            8 :     const needsFullResolution = isForImportStatementCompletion || moduleResolutionSupportsPackageJsonExportsAndImports(getEmitModuleResolutionKind(program.getCompilerOptions()));
     638            8 :     let skippedAny = false;
     639            8 :     let ambientCount = 0;
     640            8 :     let resolvedCount = 0;
     641            8 :     let resolvedFromCacheCount = 0;
     642            8 :     let cacheAttemptCount = 0;
     643            8 : 
     644            8 :     const result = cb({
     645            8 :         tryResolve,
     646            8 :         skippedAny: () => skippedAny,
     647            8 :         resolvedAny: () => resolvedCount > 0,
     648            8 :         resolvedBeyondLimit: () => resolvedCount > moduleSpecifierResolutionLimit,
     649            8 :     });
     650            8 : 
     651            8 :     const hitRateMessage = cacheAttemptCount ? ` (${(resolvedFromCacheCount / cacheAttemptCount * 100).toFixed(1)}% hit rate)` : "";
     652            8 :     host.log?.(`${logPrefix}: resolved ${resolvedCount} module specifiers, plus ${ambientCount} ambient and ${resolvedFromCacheCount} from cache${hitRateMessage}`);
     653            8 :     host.log?.(`${logPrefix}: response is ${skippedAny ? "incomplete" : "complete"}`);
     654            8 :     host.log?.(`${logPrefix}: ${timestamp() - start}`);
     655            8 :     return result;
     656            8 : 
     657            8 :     function tryResolve(exportInfo: readonly SymbolExportInfo[], isFromAmbientModule: boolean): ModuleSpecifierResolutionResult {
     658            8 :         if (isFromAmbientModule) {
     659            8 :             const result = resolver.getModuleSpecifierForBestExportInfo(exportInfo, position, isValidTypeOnlyUseSite);
     660            8 :             if (result) {
     661            8 :                 ambientCount++;
     662            8 :             }
     663            8 :             return result || "failed";
     664            8 :         }
     665            8 :         const shouldResolveModuleSpecifier = needsFullResolution || preferences.allowIncompleteCompletions && resolvedCount < moduleSpecifierResolutionLimit;
     666            8 :         const shouldGetModuleSpecifierFromCache = !shouldResolveModuleSpecifier && preferences.allowIncompleteCompletions && cacheAttemptCount < moduleSpecifierResolutionCacheAttemptLimit;
     667            8 :         const result = (shouldResolveModuleSpecifier || shouldGetModuleSpecifierFromCache)
     668            8 :             ? resolver.getModuleSpecifierForBestExportInfo(exportInfo, position, isValidTypeOnlyUseSite, shouldGetModuleSpecifierFromCache)
     669            8 :             : undefined;
     670            8 : 
     671            8 :         if (!shouldResolveModuleSpecifier && !shouldGetModuleSpecifierFromCache || shouldGetModuleSpecifierFromCache && !result) {
     672            8 :             skippedAny = true;
     673            8 :         }
     674            8 : 
     675            8 :         resolvedCount += result?.computedWithoutCacheCount || 0;
     676            8 :         resolvedFromCacheCount += exportInfo.length - (result?.computedWithoutCacheCount || 0);
     677            8 :         if (shouldGetModuleSpecifierFromCache) {
     678            8 :             cacheAttemptCount++;
     679            8 :         }
     680            8 : 
     681            8 :         return result || (needsFullResolution ? "failed" : "skipped");
     682            8 :     }
     683            8 : }
     684            8 : 
     685            8 : /** @internal */
     686            8 : export function getCompletionsAtPosition(
     687            8 :     host: LanguageServiceHost,
     688            8 :     program: Program,
     689            8 :     log: Log,
     690            8 :     sourceFile: SourceFile,
     691            8 :     position: number,
     692            8 :     preferences: UserPreferences,
     693            8 :     triggerCharacter: CompletionsTriggerCharacter | undefined,
     694            8 :     completionKind: CompletionTriggerKind | undefined,
     695            8 :     cancellationToken: CancellationToken,
     696            8 :     formatContext?: formatting.FormatContext,
     697            8 :     includeSymbol = false,
     698            8 : ): CompletionInfo | undefined {
     699            8 :     const { previousToken } = getRelevantTokens(position, sourceFile);
     700            8 :     if (triggerCharacter && !isInString(sourceFile, position, previousToken) && !isValidTrigger(sourceFile, triggerCharacter, previousToken, position)) {
     701            8 :         return undefined;
     702            8 :     }
     703            8 : 
     704            8 :     if (triggerCharacter === " ") {
     705            8 :         // `isValidTrigger` ensures we are at `import |`
     706            8 :         if (preferences.includeCompletionsForImportStatements && preferences.includeCompletionsWithInsertText) {
     707            8 :             return { isGlobalCompletion: true, isMemberCompletion: false, isNewIdentifierLocation: true, isIncomplete: true, entries: [] };
     708            8 :         }
     709            8 :         return undefined;
     710            8 :     }
     711            8 : 
     712            8 :     const compilerOptions = program.getCompilerOptions();
     713            8 :     const checker = program.getTypeChecker();
     714            8 :     // If the request is a continuation of an earlier `isIncomplete` response,
     715            8 :     // we can continue it from the cached previous response.
     716            8 :     const incompleteCompletionsCache = preferences.allowIncompleteCompletions ? host.getIncompleteCompletionsCache?.() : undefined;
     717            8 :     if (incompleteCompletionsCache && completionKind === CompletionTriggerKind.TriggerForIncompleteCompletions && previousToken && isIdentifier(previousToken)) {
     718            8 :         const incompleteContinuation = continuePreviousIncompleteResponse(incompleteCompletionsCache, sourceFile, previousToken, program, host, preferences, cancellationToken, position);
     719            8 :         if (incompleteContinuation) {
     720            8 :             return incompleteContinuation;
     721            8 :         }
     722            8 :     }
     723            8 :     else {
     724            8 :         incompleteCompletionsCache?.clear();
     725            8 :     }
     726            8 : 
     727            8 :     const stringCompletions = StringCompletions.getStringLiteralCompletions(sourceFile, position, previousToken, compilerOptions, host, program, log, preferences, includeSymbol);
     728            8 :     if (stringCompletions) {
     729            8 :         return stringCompletions;
     730            8 :     }
     731            8 : 
     732            8 :     if (
     733            8 :         previousToken && isBreakOrContinueStatement(previousToken.parent)
     734            8 :         && (previousToken.kind === SyntaxKind.BreakKeyword || previousToken.kind === SyntaxKind.ContinueKeyword || previousToken.kind === SyntaxKind.Identifier)
     735            8 :     ) {
     736            8 :         return getLabelCompletionAtPosition(previousToken.parent);
     737            8 :     }
     738            8 : 
     739            8 :     const completionData = getCompletionData(program, log, sourceFile, compilerOptions, position, preferences, /*detailsEntryId*/ undefined, host, formatContext, cancellationToken);
     740            8 :     if (!completionData) {
     741            8 :         return undefined;
     742            8 :     }
     743            8 : 
     744            8 :     switch (completionData.kind) {
     745            8 :         case CompletionDataKind.Data:
     746            8 :             const response = completionInfoFromData(sourceFile, host, program, compilerOptions, log, completionData, preferences, formatContext, position, includeSymbol);
     747            8 :             if (response?.isIncomplete) {
     748            8 :                 incompleteCompletionsCache?.set(response);
     749            8 :             }
     750            8 :             return response;
     751            8 :         case CompletionDataKind.JsDocTagName:
     752            8 :             // If the current position is a jsDoc tag name, only tag names should be provided for completion
     753            8 :             return jsdocCompletionInfo([
     754            8 :                 ...JsDoc.getJSDocTagNameCompletions(),
     755            8 :                 ...getJSDocParameterCompletions(
     756            8 :                     sourceFile,
     757            8 :                     position,
     758            8 :                     checker,
     759            8 :                     compilerOptions,
     760            8 :                     preferences,
     761            8 :                     /*tagNameOnly*/ true,
     762            8 :                 ),
     763            8 :             ]);
     764            8 :         case CompletionDataKind.JsDocTag:
     765            8 :             // If the current position is a jsDoc tag, only tags should be provided for completion
     766            8 :             return jsdocCompletionInfo([
     767            8 :                 ...JsDoc.getJSDocTagCompletions(),
     768            8 :                 ...getJSDocParameterCompletions(
     769            8 :                     sourceFile,
     770            8 :                     position,
     771            8 :                     checker,
     772            8 :                     compilerOptions,
     773            8 :                     preferences,
     774            8 :                     /*tagNameOnly*/ false,
     775            8 :                 ),
     776            8 :             ]);
     777            8 :         case CompletionDataKind.JsDocParameterName:
     778            8 :             return jsdocCompletionInfo(JsDoc.getJSDocParameterNameCompletions(completionData.tag));
     779            8 :         case CompletionDataKind.Keywords:
     780            8 :             return specificKeywordCompletionInfo(completionData.keywordCompletions, completionData.isNewIdentifierLocation);
     781            8 :         default:
     782            8 :             return Debug.assertNever(completionData);
     783            8 :     }
     784            8 : }
     785            8 : 
     786            8 : // Editors will use the `sortText` and then fall back to `name` for sorting, but leave ties in response order.
     787            8 : // So, it's important that we sort those ties in the order we want them displayed if it matters. We don't
     788            8 : // strictly need to sort by name or SortText here since clients are going to do it anyway, but we have to
     789            8 : // do the work of comparing them so we can sort those ties appropriately; plus, it makes the order returned
     790            8 : // by the language service consistent with what TS Server does and what editors typically do. This also makes
     791            8 : // completions tests make more sense. We used to sort only alphabetically and only in the server layer, but
     792            8 : // this made tests really weird, since most fourslash tests don't use the server.
     793            8 : function compareCompletionEntries(entryInArray: CompletionEntry, entryToInsert: CompletionEntry): Comparison {
     794            8 :     let result = compareStringsCaseSensitiveUI(entryInArray.sortText, entryToInsert.sortText);
     795            8 :     if (result === Comparison.EqualTo) {
     796            8 :         result = compareStringsCaseSensitiveUI(entryInArray.name, entryToInsert.name);
     797            8 :     }
     798            8 :     if (result === Comparison.EqualTo && entryInArray.data?.moduleSpecifier && entryToInsert.data?.moduleSpecifier) {
     799            8 :         // Sort same-named auto-imports by module specifier
     800            8 :         result = compareNumberOfDirectorySeparators(
     801            8 :             (entryInArray.data as CompletionEntryDataResolved).moduleSpecifier,
     802            8 :             (entryToInsert.data as CompletionEntryDataResolved).moduleSpecifier,
     803            8 :         );
     804            8 :     }
     805            8 :     if (result === Comparison.EqualTo) {
     806            8 :         // Fall back to symbol order - if we return `EqualTo`, `insertSorted` will put later symbols first.
     807            8 :         return Comparison.LessThan;
     808            8 :     }
     809            8 :     return result;
     810            8 : }
     811            8 : 
     812            8 : function completionEntryDataIsResolved(data: CompletionEntryDataAutoImport | undefined): data is CompletionEntryDataResolved {
     813            8 :     return !!data?.moduleSpecifier;
     814            8 : }
     815            8 : 
     816            8 : function continuePreviousIncompleteResponse(
     817            8 :     cache: IncompleteCompletionsCache,
     818            8 :     file: SourceFile,
     819            8 :     location: Identifier,
     820            8 :     program: Program,
     821            8 :     host: LanguageServiceHost,
     822            8 :     preferences: UserPreferences,
     823            8 :     cancellationToken: CancellationToken,
     824            8 :     position: number,
     825            8 : ): CompletionInfo | undefined {
     826            8 :     const previousResponse = cache.get();
     827            8 :     if (!previousResponse) return undefined;
     828            8 : 
     829            8 :     const touchNode = getTouchingPropertyName(file, position);
     830            8 :     const lowerCaseTokenText = location.text.toLowerCase();
     831            8 :     const exportMap = getExportInfoMap(file, host, program, preferences, cancellationToken);
     832            8 :     const newEntries = resolvingModuleSpecifiers(
     833            8 :         "continuePreviousIncompleteResponse",
     834            8 :         host,
     835            8 :         codefix.createImportSpecifierResolver(file, program, host, preferences),
     836            8 :         program,
     837            8 :         location.getStart(),
     838            8 :         preferences,
     839            8 :         /*isForImportStatementCompletion*/ false,
     840            8 :         isValidTypeOnlyAliasUseSite(location),
     841            8 :         context => {
     842            8 :             const entries = mapDefined(previousResponse.entries, entry => {
     843            8 :                 if (!entry.hasAction || !entry.source || !entry.data || completionEntryDataIsResolved(entry.data)) {
     844            8 :                     // Not an auto import or already resolved; keep as is
     845            8 :                     return entry;
     846            8 :                 }
     847            8 :                 if (!charactersFuzzyMatchInString(entry.name, lowerCaseTokenText)) {
     848            8 :                     // No longer matches typed characters; filter out
     849            8 :                     return undefined;
     850            8 :                 }
     851            8 : 
     852            8 :                 const { origin } = Debug.checkDefined(getAutoImportSymbolFromCompletionEntryData(entry.name, entry.data, program, host));
     853            8 :                 const info = exportMap.get(file.path, entry.data.exportMapKey);
     854            8 : 
     855            8 :                 const result = info && context.tryResolve(info, !isExternalModuleNameRelative(stripQuotes(origin.moduleSymbol.name)));
     856            8 :                 if (result === "skipped") return entry;
     857            8 :                 if (!result || result === "failed") {
     858            8 :                     host.log?.(`Unexpected failure resolving auto import for '${entry.name}' from '${entry.source}'`);
     859            8 :                     return undefined;
     860            8 :                 }
     861            8 : 
     862            8 :                 const newOrigin: SymbolOriginInfoResolvedExport = {
     863            8 :                     ...origin,
     864            8 :                     kind: SymbolOriginInfoKind.ResolvedExport,
     865            8 :                     moduleSpecifier: result.moduleSpecifier,
     866            8 :                 };
     867            8 :                 // Mutating for performance... feels sketchy but nobody else uses the cache,
     868            8 :                 // so why bother allocating a bunch of new objects?
     869            8 :                 entry.data = originToCompletionEntryData(newOrigin);
     870            8 :                 entry.source = getSourceFromOrigin(newOrigin);
     871            8 :                 entry.sourceDisplay = [textPart(newOrigin.moduleSpecifier)];
     872            8 :                 return entry;
     873            8 :             });
     874            8 : 
     875            8 :             if (!context.skippedAny()) {
     876            8 :                 previousResponse.isIncomplete = undefined;
     877            8 :             }
     878            8 : 
     879            8 :             return entries;
     880            8 :         },
     881            8 :     );
     882            8 : 
     883            8 :     previousResponse.entries = newEntries;
     884            8 :     previousResponse.flags = (previousResponse.flags || 0) | CompletionInfoFlags.IsContinuation;
     885            8 :     previousResponse.optionalReplacementSpan = getOptionalReplacementSpan(touchNode);
     886            8 :     return previousResponse;
     887            8 : }
     888            8 : 
     889            8 : function jsdocCompletionInfo(entries: CompletionEntry[]): CompletionInfo {
     890            8 :     return { isGlobalCompletion: false, isMemberCompletion: false, isNewIdentifierLocation: false, entries };
     891            8 : }
     892            8 : 
     893            8 : function getJSDocParameterCompletions(
     894            8 :     sourceFile: SourceFile,
     895            8 :     position: number,
     896            8 :     checker: TypeChecker,
     897            8 :     options: CompilerOptions,
     898            8 :     preferences: UserPreferences,
     899            8 :     tagNameOnly: boolean,
     900            8 : ): CompletionEntry[] {
     901            8 :     const currentToken = getTokenAtPosition(sourceFile, position);
     902            8 :     if (!isJSDocTag(currentToken) && !isJSDoc(currentToken)) {
     903            8 :         return [];
     904            8 :     }
     905            8 :     const jsDoc = isJSDoc(currentToken) ? currentToken : currentToken.parent;
     906            8 :     if (!isJSDoc(jsDoc)) {
     907            8 :         return [];
     908            8 :     }
     909            8 :     const func = jsDoc.parent;
     910            8 :     if (!isFunctionLike(func)) {
     911            8 :         return [];
     912            8 :     }
     913            8 : 
     914            8 :     const isJs = isSourceFileJS(sourceFile);
     915            8 :     const isSnippet = preferences.includeCompletionsWithSnippetText || undefined;
     916            8 :     const paramTagCount = countWhere(jsDoc.tags, tag => isJSDocParameterTag(tag) && tag.getEnd() <= position);
     917            8 :     return mapDefined(func.parameters, param => {
     918            8 :         if (getJSDocParameterTags(param).length) {
     919            8 :             return undefined; // Parameter is already annotated.
     920            8 :         }
     921            8 :         if (isIdentifier(param.name)) { // Named parameter
     922            8 :             const tabstopCounter = { tabstop: 1 };
     923            8 :             const paramName = param.name.text;
     924            8 :             let displayText = getJSDocParamAnnotation(
     925            8 :                 paramName,
     926            8 :                 param.initializer,
     927            8 :                 param.dotDotDotToken,
     928            8 :                 isJs,
     929            8 :                 /*isObject*/ false,
     930            8 :                 /*isSnippet*/ false,
     931            8 :                 checker,
     932            8 :                 options,
     933            8 :                 preferences,
     934            8 :             );
     935            8 :             let snippetText = isSnippet
     936            8 :                 ? getJSDocParamAnnotation(
     937            8 :                     paramName,
     938            8 :                     param.initializer,
     939            8 :                     param.dotDotDotToken,
     940            8 :                     isJs,
     941            8 :                     /*isObject*/ false,
     942            8 :                     /*isSnippet*/ true,
     943            8 :                     checker,
     944            8 :                     options,
     945            8 :                     preferences,
     946            8 :                     tabstopCounter,
     947            8 :                 )
     948            8 :                 : undefined;
     949            8 :             if (tagNameOnly) { // Remove `@`
     950            8 :                 displayText = displayText.slice(1);
     951            8 :                 if (snippetText) snippetText = snippetText.slice(1);
     952            8 :             }
     953            8 :             return {
     954            8 :                 name: displayText,
     955            8 :                 kind: ScriptElementKind.parameterElement,
     956            8 :                 sortText: SortText.LocationPriority,
     957            8 :                 insertText: isSnippet ? snippetText : undefined,
     958            8 :                 isSnippet,
     959            8 :             };
     960            8 :         }
     961            8 :         else if (param.parent.parameters.indexOf(param) === paramTagCount) { // Destructuring parameter; do it positionally
     962            8 :             const paramPath = `param${paramTagCount}`;
     963            8 :             const displayTextResult = generateJSDocParamTagsForDestructuring(
     964            8 :                 paramPath,
     965            8 :                 param.name,
     966            8 :                 param.initializer,
     967            8 :                 param.dotDotDotToken,
     968            8 :                 isJs,
     969            8 :                 /*isSnippet*/ false,
     970            8 :                 checker,
     971            8 :                 options,
     972            8 :                 preferences,
     973            8 :             );
     974            8 :             const snippetTextResult = isSnippet
     975            8 :                 ? generateJSDocParamTagsForDestructuring(
     976            8 :                     paramPath,
     977            8 :                     param.name,
     978            8 :                     param.initializer,
     979            8 :                     param.dotDotDotToken,
     980            8 :                     isJs,
     981            8 :                     /*isSnippet*/ true,
     982            8 :                     checker,
     983            8 :                     options,
     984            8 :                     preferences,
     985            8 :                 )
     986            8 :                 : undefined;
     987            8 :             let displayText = displayTextResult.join(getNewLineCharacter(options) + "* ");
     988            8 :             let snippetText = snippetTextResult?.join(getNewLineCharacter(options) + "* ");
     989            8 :             if (tagNameOnly) { // Remove `@`
     990            8 :                 displayText = displayText.slice(1);
     991            8 :                 if (snippetText) snippetText = snippetText.slice(1);
     992            8 :             }
     993            8 :             return {
     994            8 :                 name: displayText,
     995            8 :                 kind: ScriptElementKind.parameterElement,
     996            8 :                 sortText: SortText.LocationPriority,
     997            8 :                 insertText: isSnippet ? snippetText : undefined,
     998            8 :                 isSnippet,
     999            8 :             };
    1000            8 :         }
    1001            8 :     });
    1002            8 : }
    1003            8 : 
    1004            8 : function generateJSDocParamTagsForDestructuring(
    1005            8 :     path: string,
    1006            8 :     pattern: BindingPattern,
    1007            8 :     initializer: Expression | undefined,
    1008            8 :     dotDotDotToken: DotDotDotToken | undefined,
    1009            8 :     isJs: boolean,
    1010            8 :     isSnippet: boolean,
    1011            8 :     checker: TypeChecker,
    1012            8 :     options: CompilerOptions,
    1013            8 :     preferences: UserPreferences,
    1014            8 : ): string[] {
    1015            8 :     if (!isJs) {
    1016            8 :         return [
    1017            8 :             getJSDocParamAnnotation(
    1018            8 :                 path,
    1019            8 :                 initializer,
    1020            8 :                 dotDotDotToken,
    1021            8 :                 isJs,
    1022            8 :                 /*isObject*/ false,
    1023            8 :                 isSnippet,
    1024            8 :                 checker,
    1025            8 :                 options,
    1026            8 :                 preferences,
    1027            8 :                 { tabstop: 1 },
    1028            8 :             ),
    1029            8 :         ];
    1030            8 :     }
    1031            8 :     return patternWorker(path, pattern, initializer, dotDotDotToken, { tabstop: 1 });
    1032            8 : 
    1033            8 :     function patternWorker(
    1034            8 :         path: string,
    1035            8 :         pattern: BindingPattern,
    1036            8 :         initializer: Expression | undefined,
    1037            8 :         dotDotDotToken: DotDotDotToken | undefined,
    1038            8 :         counter: TabStopCounter,
    1039            8 :     ): string[] {
    1040            8 :         if (isObjectBindingPattern(pattern) && !dotDotDotToken) {
    1041            8 :             const oldTabstop = counter.tabstop;
    1042            8 :             const childCounter = { tabstop: oldTabstop };
    1043            8 :             const rootParam = getJSDocParamAnnotation(
    1044            8 :                 path,
    1045            8 :                 initializer,
    1046            8 :                 dotDotDotToken,
    1047            8 :                 isJs,
    1048            8 :                 /*isObject*/ true,
    1049            8 :                 isSnippet,
    1050            8 :                 checker,
    1051            8 :                 options,
    1052            8 :                 preferences,
    1053            8 :                 childCounter,
    1054            8 :             );
    1055            8 :             let childTags: string[] | undefined = [];
    1056            8 :             for (const element of pattern.elements) {
    1057            8 :                 const elementTags = elementWorker(path, element, childCounter);
    1058            8 :                 if (!elementTags) {
    1059            8 :                     childTags = undefined;
    1060            8 :                     break;
    1061            8 :                 }
    1062            8 :                 else {
    1063            8 :                     childTags.push(...elementTags);
    1064            8 :                 }
    1065            8 :             }
    1066            8 :             if (childTags) {
    1067            8 :                 counter.tabstop = childCounter.tabstop;
    1068            8 :                 return [rootParam, ...childTags];
    1069            8 :             }
    1070            8 :         }
    1071            8 :         return [
    1072            8 :             getJSDocParamAnnotation(
    1073            8 :                 path,
    1074            8 :                 initializer,
    1075            8 :                 dotDotDotToken,
    1076            8 :                 isJs,
    1077            8 :                 /*isObject*/ false,
    1078            8 :                 isSnippet,
    1079            8 :                 checker,
    1080            8 :                 options,
    1081            8 :                 preferences,
    1082            8 :                 counter,
    1083            8 :             ),
    1084            8 :         ];
    1085            8 :     }
    1086            8 : 
    1087            8 :     // Assumes binding element is inside object binding pattern.
    1088            8 :     // We can't really deeply annotate an array binding pattern.
    1089            8 :     function elementWorker(path: string, element: BindingElement, counter: TabStopCounter): string[] | undefined {
    1090            8 :         if ((!element.propertyName && isIdentifier(element.name)) || isIdentifier(element.name)) { // `{ b }` or `{ b: newB }`
    1091            8 :             const propertyName = element.propertyName ? tryGetTextOfPropertyName(element.propertyName) : element.name.text;
    1092            8 :             if (!propertyName) {
    1093            8 :                 return undefined;
    1094            8 :             }
    1095            8 :             const paramName = `${path}.${propertyName}`;
    1096            8 :             return [
    1097            8 :                 getJSDocParamAnnotation(
    1098            8 :                     paramName,
    1099            8 :                     element.initializer,
    1100            8 :                     element.dotDotDotToken,
    1101            8 :                     isJs,
    1102            8 :                     /*isObject*/ false,
    1103            8 :                     isSnippet,
    1104            8 :                     checker,
    1105            8 :                     options,
    1106            8 :                     preferences,
    1107            8 :                     counter,
    1108            8 :                 ),
    1109            8 :             ];
    1110            8 :         }
    1111            8 :         else if (element.propertyName) { // `{ b: {...} }` or `{ b: [...] }`
    1112            8 :             const propertyName = tryGetTextOfPropertyName(element.propertyName);
    1113            8 :             return propertyName
    1114            8 :                 && patternWorker(`${path}.${propertyName}`, element.name, element.initializer, element.dotDotDotToken, counter);
    1115            8 :         }
    1116            8 :         return undefined;
    1117            8 :     }
    1118            8 : }

    1120            8 : interface TabStopCounter {
    1121            8 :     tabstop: number;

    1123            8 : 
    1124            8 : function getJSDocParamAnnotation(
    1125            8 :     paramName: string,
    1126            8 :     initializer: Expression | undefined,
    1127            8 :     dotDotDotToken: DotDotDotToken | undefined,
    1128            8 :     isJs: boolean,
    1129            8 :     isObject: boolean,
    1130            8 :     isSnippet: boolean,
    1131            8 :     checker: TypeChecker,
    1132            8 :     options: CompilerOptions,
    1133            8 :     preferences: UserPreferences,
    1134            8 :     tabstopCounter?: TabStopCounter,
    1135            8 : ) {
    1136            8 :     if (isSnippet) {
    1137            8 :         Debug.assertIsDefined(tabstopCounter);
    1138            8 :     }
    1139            8 :     if (initializer) {
    1140            8 :         paramName = getJSDocParamNameWithInitializer(paramName, initializer);
    1141            8 :     }
    1142            8 :     if (isSnippet) {
    1143            8 :         paramName = escapeSnippetText(paramName);
    1144            8 :     }
    1145            8 :     if (isJs) {
    1146            8 :         let type = "*";
    1147            8 :         if (isObject) {
    1148            8 :             Debug.assert(!dotDotDotToken, `Cannot annotate a rest parameter with type 'Object'.`);
    1149            8 :             type = "Object";
    1150            8 :         }
    1151            8 :         else {
    1152            8 :             if (initializer) {
    1153            8 :                 const inferredType = checker.getTypeAtLocation(initializer.parent);
    1154            8 :                 if (!(inferredType.flags & (TypeFlags.Any | TypeFlags.Void))) {
    1155            8 :                     const sourceFile = initializer.getSourceFile();
    1156            8 :                     const quotePreference = getQuotePreference(sourceFile, preferences);
    1157            8 :                     const builderFlags = quotePreference === QuotePreference.Single ? NodeBuilderFlags.UseSingleQuotesForStringLiteralType : NodeBuilderFlags.None;
    1158            8 :                     const typeNode = checker.typeToTypeNode(inferredType, findAncestor(initializer, isFunctionLike), builderFlags);
    1159            8 :                     if (typeNode) {
    1160            8 :                         const printer = isSnippet
    1161            8 :                             ? createSnippetPrinter({
    1162            8 :                                 removeComments: true,
    1163            8 :                                 module: options.module,
    1164            8 :                                 moduleResolution: options.moduleResolution,
    1165            8 :                                 target: options.target,
    1166            8 :                             })
    1167            8 :                             : createPrinter({
    1168            8 :                                 removeComments: true,
    1169            8 :                                 module: options.module,
    1170            8 :                                 moduleResolution: options.moduleResolution,
    1171            8 :                                 target: options.target,
    1172            8 :                             });
    1173            8 :                         setEmitFlags(typeNode, EmitFlags.SingleLine);
    1174            8 :                         type = printer.printNode(EmitHint.Unspecified, typeNode, sourceFile);
    1175            8 :                     }
    1176            8 :                 }
    1177            8 :             }
    1178            8 :             if (isSnippet && type === "*") {
    1179            8 :                 type = `\${${tabstopCounter!.tabstop++}:${type}}`;
    1180            8 :             }
    1181            8 :         }
    1182            8 :         const dotDotDot = !isObject && dotDotDotToken ? "..." : "";
    1183            8 :         const description = isSnippet ? `\${${tabstopCounter!.tabstop++}}` : "";
    1184            8 :         return `@param {${dotDotDot}${type}} ${paramName} ${description}`;
    1185            8 :     }
    1186            8 :     else {
    1187            8 :         const description = isSnippet ? `\${${tabstopCounter!.tabstop++}}` : "";
    1188            8 :         return `@param ${paramName} ${description}`;
    1189            8 :     }
    1190            8 : }
    1191            8 : 
    1192            8 : function getJSDocParamNameWithInitializer(paramName: string, initializer: Expression): string {
    1193            8 :     const initializerText = initializer.getText().trim();
    1194            8 :     if (initializerText.includes("\n") || initializerText.length > 80) {
    1195            8 :         return `[${paramName}]`;
    1196            8 :     }
    1197            8 :     return `[${paramName}=${initializerText}]`;
    1198            8 : }

    1275            8 :     const checker = program.getTypeChecker();

    1277            8 :     // Verify if the file is JSX language variant

    1279            8 :         const completionInfo = getJsxClosingTagCompletion(location, sourceFile);
    1280            8 :         if (completionInfo) {

    1285            8 :     // When the completion is for the expression of a case clause (e.g. `case |`),
    1286            8 :     // filter literals & enum symbols whose values are already present in existing case clauses.
    1287            8 :     const caseClause = findAncestor(contextToken, isCaseClause);

    1289            8 :         const tracker = newCaseClauseTracker(checker, caseClause.parent.clauses);
    1290            8 :         literals = literals.filter(literal => !tracker.hasValue(literal));
    1291            8 :         // The `symbols` array cannot be filtered directly, because to each symbol at position i in `symbols`,
    1292            8 :         // there might be a corresponding origin at position i in `symbolToOriginInfoMap`.
    1293            8 :         // So instead of filtering the `symbols` array, we mark symbols to be ignored.
    1294            8 :         symbols.forEach((symbol, i) => {
    1295            8 :             if (symbol.valueDeclaration && isEnumMember(symbol.valueDeclaration)) {
    1296            8 :                 const value = checker.getConstantValue(symbol.valueDeclaration);
    1297            8 :                 if (value !== undefined && tracker.hasValue(value)) {
    1298            8 :                     symbolToOriginInfoMap[i] = { kind: SymbolOriginInfoKind.Ignore };
    1299            8 :                 }
    1300            8 :             }
    1301            8 :         });
    1302            8 :     }
    1303            8 : 
    1304            8 :     const entries = createSortedArray<CompletionEntry>();
    1305            8 :     const isChecked = isCheckedFile(sourceFile, compilerOptions);
    1306            8 :     if (isChecked && !isNewIdentifierLocation && (!symbols || symbols.length === 0) && keywordFilters === KeywordCompletionFilters.None) {
    1307            8 :         return undefined;
    1308            8 :     }
    1309            8 :     const uniqueNames = getCompletionEntriesFromSymbols(
    1310            8 :         symbols,
    1311            8 :         entries,
    1312            8 :         /*replacementToken*/ undefined,
    1313            8 :         contextToken,
    1314            8 :         location,
    1315            8 :         position,
    1316            8 :         sourceFile,
    1317            8 :         host,
    1318            8 :         program,
    1319            8 :         getEmitScriptTarget(compilerOptions),
    1320            8 :         log,
    1321            8 :         completionKind,
    1322            8 :         preferences,
    1323            8 :         compilerOptions,
    1324            8 :         formatContext,
    1325            8 :         isTypeOnlyLocation,
    1326            8 :         propertyAccessToConvert,
    1327            8 :         isJsxIdentifierExpected,
    1328            8 :         isJsxInitializer,
    1329            8 :         importStatementCompletion,
    1330            8 :         recommendedCompletion,
    1331            8 :         symbolToOriginInfoMap,
    1332            8 :         symbolToSortTextMap,
    1333            8 :         isJsxIdentifierExpected,
    1334            8 :         isRightOfOpenTag,
    1335            8 :         includeSymbol,
    1336            8 :     );
    1337            8 : 
    1338            8 :     if (keywordFilters !== KeywordCompletionFilters.None) {
    1339            8 :         for (const keywordEntry of getKeywordCompletions(keywordFilters, !insideJsDocTagTypeExpression && isSourceFileJS(sourceFile))) {
    1340            8 :             if (
    1341            8 :                 isTypeOnlyLocation && isTypeKeyword(stringToToken(keywordEntry.name)!) ||
    1342            8 :                 !isTypeOnlyLocation && isContextualKeywordInAutoImportableExpressionSpace(keywordEntry.name) ||
    1343            8 :                 !uniqueNames.has(keywordEntry.name)
    1344            8 :             ) {
    1345            8 :                 uniqueNames.add(keywordEntry.name);
    1346            8 :                 insertSorted(entries, keywordEntry, compareCompletionEntries, /*equalityComparer*/ undefined, /*allowDuplicates*/ true);
    1347            8 :             }
    1348            8 :         }
    1349            8 :     }
    1350            8 : 
    1351            8 :     for (const keywordEntry of getContextualKeywords(contextToken, position)) {
    1352            8 :         if (!uniqueNames.has(keywordEntry.name)) {
    1353            8 :             uniqueNames.add(keywordEntry.name);
    1354            8 :             insertSorted(entries, keywordEntry, compareCompletionEntries, /*equalityComparer*/ undefined, /*allowDuplicates*/ true);
    1355            8 :         }
    1356            8 :     }
    1357            8 : 
    1358            8 :     for (const literal of literals) {
    1359            8 :         const literalEntry = createCompletionEntryForLiteral(sourceFile, preferences, literal);
    1360            8 :         uniqueNames.add(literalEntry.name);
    1361            8 :         insertSorted(entries, literalEntry, compareCompletionEntries, /*equalityComparer*/ undefined, /*allowDuplicates*/ true);
    1362            8 :     }
    1363            8 : 
    1364            8 :     if (!isChecked) {
    1365            8 :         getJSCompletionEntries(sourceFile, location.pos, uniqueNames, getEmitScriptTarget(compilerOptions), entries);
    1366            8 :     }
    1367            8 : 
    1368            8 :     let caseBlock: CaseBlock | undefined;
    1369            8 :     if (
    1370            8 :         preferences.includeCompletionsWithInsertText
    1371            8 :         && contextToken
    1372            8 :         && !isRightOfOpenTag
    1373            8 :         && !isRightOfDotOrQuestionDot
    1374            8 :         && (caseBlock = findAncestor(contextToken, isCaseBlock))
    1375            8 :     ) {
    1376            8 :         const cases = getExhaustiveCaseSnippets(caseBlock, sourceFile, preferences, compilerOptions, host, program, formatContext);
    1377            8 :         if (cases) {
    1378            8 :             entries.push(cases.entry);
    1379            8 :         }
    1380            8 :     }

    1386            8 :         isMemberCompletion: isMemberCompletionKind(completionKind),
    1387            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation,

    1389            8 :         entries,
    1390            8 :     };
    1391            8 : }

    1393            8 : function isCheckedFile(sourceFile: SourceFile, compilerOptions: CompilerOptions): boolean {
    1394            8 :     return !isSourceFileJS(sourceFile) || !!isCheckJsEnabledForFile(sourceFile, compilerOptions);
    1395            8 : }
    1396            8 : 
    1397            8 : function getExhaustiveCaseSnippets(
    1398            8 :     caseBlock: CaseBlock,
    1399            8 :     sourceFile: SourceFile,
    1400            8 :     preferences: UserPreferences,
    1401            8 :     options: CompilerOptions,
    1402            8 :     host: LanguageServiceHost,
    1403            8 :     program: Program,
    1404            8 :     formatContext: formatting.FormatContext | undefined,
    1405            8 : ): { entry: CompletionEntry; importAdder: codefix.ImportAdder; } | undefined {
    1406            8 :     const clauses = caseBlock.clauses;
    1407            8 :     const checker = program.getTypeChecker();
    1408            8 :     const switchType = checker.getTypeAtLocation(caseBlock.parent.expression);
    1409            8 :     if (switchType && switchType.isUnion() && every(switchType.types, type => type.isLiteral())) {
    1410            8 :         // Collect constant values in existing clauses.
    1411            8 :         const tracker = newCaseClauseTracker(checker, clauses);
    1412            8 : 
    1413            8 :         const target = getEmitScriptTarget(options);
    1414            8 :         const quotePreference = getQuotePreference(sourceFile, preferences);
    1415            8 :         const importAdder = codefix.createImportAdder(sourceFile, program, preferences, host);
    1416            8 :         const elements: Expression[] = [];
    1417            8 :         for (const type of switchType.types as LiteralType[]) {
    1418            8 :             // Enums
    1419            8 :             if (type.flags & TypeFlags.EnumLiteral) {
    1420            8 :                 Debug.assert(type.symbol, "An enum member type should have a symbol");
    1421            8 :                 Debug.assert(type.symbol.parent, "An enum member type should have a parent symbol (the enum symbol)");
    1422            8 :                 // Filter existing enums by their values
    1423            8 :                 const enumValue = type.symbol.valueDeclaration && checker.getConstantValue(type.symbol.valueDeclaration as EnumMember);
    1424            8 :                 if (enumValue !== undefined) {
    1425            8 :                     if (tracker.hasValue(enumValue)) {
    1426            8 :                         continue;
    1427            8 :                     }
    1428            8 :                     tracker.addValue(enumValue);
    1429            8 :                 }
    1430            8 :                 const typeNode = codefix.typeToAutoImportableTypeNode(checker, importAdder, type, caseBlock, target);
    1431            8 :                 if (!typeNode) {
    1432            8 :                     return undefined;
    1433            8 :                 }
    1434            8 :                 const expr = typeNodeToExpression(typeNode, target, quotePreference);
    1435            8 :                 if (!expr) {
    1436            8 :                     return undefined;
    1437            8 :                 }
    1438            8 :                 elements.push(expr);
    1439            8 :             }
    1440            8 :             // Literals
    1441            8 :             else if (!tracker.hasValue(type.value)) {
    1442            8 :                 switch (typeof type.value) {
    1443            8 :                     case "object":
    1444            8 :                         elements.push(type.value.negative ? factory.createPrefixUnaryExpression(SyntaxKind.MinusToken, factory.createBigIntLiteral({ negative: false, base10Value: type.value.base10Value })) : factory.createBigIntLiteral(type.value));
    1445            8 :                         break;
    1446            8 :                     case "number":
    1447            8 :                         elements.push(type.value < 0 ? factory.createPrefixUnaryExpression(SyntaxKind.MinusToken, factory.createNumericLiteral(-type.value)) : factory.createNumericLiteral(type.value));
    1448            8 :                         break;
    1449            8 :                     case "string":
    1450            8 :                         elements.push(factory.createStringLiteral(type.value, quotePreference === QuotePreference.Single));
    1451            8 :                         break;
    1452            8 :                 }
    1453            8 :             }
    1454            8 :         }
    1455            8 :         if (elements.length === 0) {
    1456            8 :             return undefined;
    1457            8 :         }
    1458            8 : 
    1459            8 :         const newClauses = map(elements, element => factory.createCaseClause(element, []));
    1460            8 :         const newLineChar = getNewLineOrDefaultFromHost(host, formatContext?.options);
    1461            8 :         const printer = createSnippetPrinter({
    1462            8 :             removeComments: true,
    1463            8 :             module: options.module,
    1464            8 :             moduleResolution: options.moduleResolution,
    1465            8 :             target: options.target,
    1466            8 :             newLine: getNewLineKind(newLineChar),
    1467            8 :         });
    1468            8 :         const printNode = formatContext
    1469            8 :             ? (node: Node) => printer.printAndFormatNode(EmitHint.Unspecified, node, sourceFile, formatContext)
    1470            8 :             : (node: Node) => printer.printNode(EmitHint.Unspecified, node, sourceFile);
    1471            8 :         const insertText = map(newClauses, (clause, i) => {
    1472            8 :             if (preferences.includeCompletionsWithSnippetText) {
    1473            8 :                 return `${printNode(clause)}$${i + 1}`;
    1474            8 :             }
    1475            8 :             return `${printNode(clause)}`;
    1476            8 :         }).join(newLineChar);
    1477            8 : 
    1478            8 :         const firstClause = printer.printNode(EmitHint.Unspecified, newClauses[0], sourceFile);
    1479            8 :         return {
    1480            8 :             entry: {
    1481            8 :                 name: `${firstClause} ...`,
    1482            8 :                 kind: ScriptElementKind.unknown,
    1483            8 :                 sortText: SortText.GlobalsOrKeywords,
    1484            8 :                 insertText,
    1485            8 :                 hasAction: importAdder.hasFixes() || undefined,
    1486            8 :                 source: CompletionSource.SwitchCases,
    1487            8 :                 isSnippet: preferences.includeCompletionsWithSnippetText ? true : undefined,
    1488            8 :             },
    1489            8 :             importAdder,
    1490            8 :         };
    1491            8 :     }
    1492            8 : 
    1493            8 :     return undefined;
    1494            8 : }
    1495            8 : 
    1496            8 : function typeNodeToExpression(typeNode: TypeNode, languageVersion: ScriptTarget, quotePreference: QuotePreference): Expression | undefined {
    1497            8 :     switch (typeNode.kind) {
    1498            8 :         case SyntaxKind.TypeReference:
    1499            8 :             const typeName = (typeNode as TypeReferenceNode).typeName;
    1500            8 :             return entityNameToExpression(typeName, languageVersion, quotePreference);
    1501            8 :         case SyntaxKind.IndexedAccessType:
    1502            8 :             const objectExpression = typeNodeToExpression((typeNode as IndexedAccessTypeNode).objectType, languageVersion, quotePreference);
    1503            8 :             const indexExpression = typeNodeToExpression((typeNode as IndexedAccessTypeNode).indexType, languageVersion, quotePreference);
    1504            8 :             return objectExpression
    1505            8 :                 && indexExpression
    1506            8 :                 && factory.createElementAccessExpression(objectExpression, indexExpression);
    1507            8 :         case SyntaxKind.LiteralType:
    1508            8 :             const literal = (typeNode as LiteralTypeNode).literal;
    1509            8 :             switch (literal.kind) {
    1510            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.StringLiteral:
    1511            8 :                     return factory.createStringLiteral(literal.text, quotePreference === QuotePreference.Single);
    1512            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.NumericLiteral:
    1513            8 :                     return factory.createNumericLiteral(literal.text, (literal as NumericLiteral).numericLiteralFlags);
    1514            8 :             }
    1515            8 :             return undefined;
    1516            8 :         case SyntaxKind.ParenthesizedType:
    1517            8 :             const exp = typeNodeToExpression((typeNode as ParenthesizedTypeNode).type, languageVersion, quotePreference);
    1518            8 :             return exp && (isIdentifier(exp) ? exp : factory.createParenthesizedExpression(exp));
    1519            8 :         case SyntaxKind.TypeQuery:
    1520            8 :             return entityNameToExpression((typeNode as TypeQueryNode).exprName, languageVersion, quotePreference);
    1521            8 :         case SyntaxKind.ImportType:
    1522            8 :             Debug.fail(`We should not get an import type after calling 'codefix.typeToAutoImportableTypeNode'.`);
    1523            8 :     }
    1524            8 : 
    1525            8 :     return undefined;
    1526            8 : }
    1527            8 : 
    1528            8 : function entityNameToExpression(entityName: EntityName, languageVersion: ScriptTarget, quotePreference: QuotePreference): Expression {
    1529            8 :     if (isIdentifier(entityName)) {
    1530            8 :         return entityName;
    1531            8 :     }
    1532            8 :     const unescapedName = unescapeLeadingUnderscores(entityName.right.escapedText);
    1533            8 :     if (canUsePropertyAccess(unescapedName, languageVersion)) {
    1534            8 :         return factory.createPropertyAccessExpression(
    1535            8 :             entityNameToExpression(entityName.left, languageVersion, quotePreference),
    1536            8 :             unescapedName,
    1537            8 :         );
    1538            8 :     }
    1539            8 :     else {
    1540            8 :         return factory.createElementAccessExpression(
    1541            8 :             entityNameToExpression(entityName.left, languageVersion, quotePreference),
    1542            8 :             factory.createStringLiteral(unescapedName, quotePreference === QuotePreference.Single),
    1543            8 :         );
    1544            8 :     }
    1545            8 : }
    1546            8 : 
    1547            8 : function isMemberCompletionKind(kind: CompletionKind): boolean {
    1548            8 :     switch (kind) {
    1549            8 :         case CompletionKind.ObjectPropertyDeclaration:
    1550            8 :         case CompletionKind.MemberLike:
    1551            8 :         case CompletionKind.PropertyAccess:
    1552            8 :             return true;
    1553            8 :         default:
    1554            8 :             return false;
    1555            8 :     }
    1556            8 : }

    1558            8 : function getJsxClosingTagCompletion(location: Node | undefined, sourceFile: SourceFile): CompletionInfo | undefined {
    1559            8 :     // We wanna walk up the tree till we find a JSX closing element
    1560            8 :     const jsxClosingElement = findAncestor(location, node => {
    1561            8 :         switch (node.kind) {
    1562            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JsxClosingElement:
    1563            8 :                 return true;
    1564            8 :             case SyntaxKind.SlashToken:
    1565            8 :             case SyntaxKind.GreaterThanToken:
    1566            8 :             case SyntaxKind.Identifier:
    1567            8 :             case SyntaxKind.PropertyAccessExpression:
    1568            8 :                 return false;
    1569            8 :             default:
    1570            8 :                 return "quit";
    1571            8 :         }
    1572            8 :     }) as JsxClosingElement | undefined;
    1573            8 : 
    1574            8 :     if (jsxClosingElement) {
    1575            8 :         // In the TypeScript JSX element, if such element is not defined. When users query for completion at closing tag,
    1576            8 :         // instead of simply giving unknown value, the completion will return the tag-name of an associated opening-element.
    1577            8 :         // For example:
    1578            8 :         //     var x = <div> </ /*1*/
    1579            8 :         // The completion list at "1" will contain "div>" with type any
    1580            8 :         // And at `<div> </ /*1*/ >` (with a closing `>`), the completion list will contain "div".
    1581            8 :         // And at property access expressions `<MainComponent.Child> </MainComponent. /*1*/ >` the completion will
    1582            8 :         // return full closing tag with an optional replacement span
    1583            8 :         // For example:
    1584            8 :         //     var x = <MainComponent.Child> </     MainComponent /*1*/  >
    1585            8 :         //     var y = <MainComponent.Child> </   /*2*/   MainComponent >
    1586            8 :         // the completion list at "1" and "2" will contain "MainComponent.Child" with a replacement span of closing tag name
    1587            8 :         const hasClosingAngleBracket = !!findChildOfKind(jsxClosingElement, SyntaxKind.GreaterThanToken, sourceFile);
    1588            8 :         const tagName = jsxClosingElement.parent.openingElement.tagName;
    1589            8 :         const closingTag = tagName.getText(sourceFile);
    1590            8 :         const fullClosingTag = closingTag + (hasClosingAngleBracket ? "" : ">");
    1591            8 :         const replacementSpan = createTextSpanFromNode(jsxClosingElement.tagName);
    1592            8 : 
    1593            8 :         const entry: CompletionEntry = {
    1594            8 :             name: fullClosingTag,
    1595            8 :             kind: ScriptElementKind.classElement,
    1596            8 :             kindModifiers: undefined,
    1597            8 :             sortText: SortText.LocationPriority,
    1598            8 :         };
    1599            8 :         return { isGlobalCompletion: false, isMemberCompletion: true, isNewIdentifierLocation: false, optionalReplacementSpan: replacementSpan, entries: [entry] };
    1600            8 :     }
    1601            8 :     return;
    1602            8 : }

    1604            8 : function getJSCompletionEntries(
    1605            8 :     sourceFile: SourceFile,

    1624            8 :                 isFromUncheckedFile: true,
    1625            8 :             }, compareCompletionEntries);

    1639            8 : function createCompletionEntry(

    1675            8 :     const typeChecker = program.getTypeChecker();
    1676            8 :     const insertQuestionDot = origin && originIsNullableMember(origin);

    1683            8 :     // We should only have needsConvertPropertyAccess if there's a property access to convert. But see #21790.
    1684            8 :     // Somehow there was a global with a non-identifier name. Hopefully someone will complain about getting a "foo bar" global completion and provide a repro.
    1685            8 :     else if ((useBraces || insertQuestionDot) && propertyAccessToConvert) {

    1699            8 :     }
    1700            8 : 
    1701            8 :     if (isJsxInitializer) {

    1703            8 :         insertText = `{${insertText}}`;

    1706            8 :         }
    1707            8 :     }
    1708            8 :     if (origin && originIsPromise(origin) && propertyAccessToConvert) {

    1719            8 :         const wrapNode = isInAwaitExpression ? propertyAccessToConvert.parent : propertyAccessToConvert.expression;

    1727            8 :             isSnippet = preferences.includeCompletionsWithSnippetText ? true : undefined;
    1728            8 :         }
    1729            8 :     }
    1730            8 : 
    1731            8 :     if (origin?.kind === SymbolOriginInfoKind.TypeOnlyAlias) {
    1732            8 :         hasAction = true;
    1733            8 :     }
    1734            8 : 
    1735            8 :     // Provide object member completions when missing commas, and insert missing commas.
    1736            8 :     // For example:
    1737            8 :     //

    1739            8 :     //        a: string;
    1740            8 :     //        b: number

    1786            8 :         else {
    1787            8 :             return undefined; // Skip this entry
    1788            8 :         }
    1789            8 :     }
    1790            8 :

    1801            8 :     if (
    1802            8 :         isJsxIdentifierExpected && !isRightOfOpenTag

    1860            8 :     // really we should consider passing the meaning for the node so that we don't report

    1862            8 :     // 'getSymbolModifiers' does, which is to use the first declaration.
    1863            8 :
