    1886            8 : 
    1887            8 : function generateIdentifierForArbitraryString(text: string, languageVersion: ScriptTarget | undefined): string {
    1888            8 :     let needsUnderscore = false;
    1889            8 :     let identifier = "";
    1890            8 :     let ch: number | undefined;
    1891            8 : 
    1892            8 :     // Convert "(example, text)" into "_example_text_"
    1893            8 :     for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i += ch !== undefined && ch >= 0x10000 ? 2 : 1) {
    1894            8 :         ch = text.codePointAt(i);
    1895            8 :         if (ch !== undefined && (i === 0 ? isIdentifierStart(ch, languageVersion) : isIdentifierPart(ch, languageVersion))) {
    1896            8 :             if (needsUnderscore) identifier += "_";
    1897            8 :             identifier += String.fromCodePoint(ch);
    1898            8 :             needsUnderscore = false;
    1899            8 :         }
    1900            8 :         else {
    1901            8 :             needsUnderscore = true;
    1902            8 :         }
    1903            8 :     }
    1904            8 :     if (needsUnderscore) identifier += "_";
    1905            8 : 
    1906            8 :     // Default to "_" if the provided text was empty
    1907            8 :     return identifier || "_";
    1908            8 : }
    1909            8 : 
    1910            8 : function isClassLikeMemberCompletion(symbol: Symbol, location: Node, sourceFile: SourceFile): boolean {
    1911            8 :     // TODO: support JS files.
    1912            8 :     if (isInJSFile(location)) {
    1913            8 :         return false;
    1914            8 :     }
    1915            8 : 
    1916            8 :     // Completion symbol must be for a class member.
    1917            8 :     const memberFlags = SymbolFlags.ClassMember
    1918            8 :         & SymbolFlags.EnumMemberExcludes;
    1919            8 :     /* In
    1920            8 :     `class C {
    1921            8 :         |
    1922            8 :     }`
    1923            8 :     `location` is a class-like declaration.
    1924            8 :     In
    1925            8 :     `class C {
    1926            8 :         m|
    1927            8 :     }`
    1928            8 :     `location` is an identifier,
    1929            8 :     `location.parent` is a class element declaration,
    1930            8 :     and `location.parent.parent` is a class-like declaration.
    1931            8 :     In
    1932            8 :     `abstract class C {
    1933            8 :         abstract
    1934            8 :         abstract m|
    1935            8 :     }`
    1936            8 :     `location` is a syntax list (with modifiers as children),
    1937            8 :     and `location.parent` is a class-like declaration.
    1938            8 :     */
    1939            8 :     return !!(symbol.flags & memberFlags) &&
    1940            8 :         (
    1941            8 :             isClassLike(location) ||
    1942            8 :             (
    1943            8 :                 location.parent &&
    1944            8 :                 location.parent.parent &&
    1945            8 :                 isClassElement(location.parent) &&
    1946            8 :                 location === location.parent.name &&
    1947            8 :                 location.parent.getLastToken(sourceFile) === location.parent.name &&
    1948            8 :                 isClassLike(location.parent.parent)
    1949            8 :             ) ||
    1950            8 :             (
    1951            8 :                 location.parent &&
    1952            8 :                 isSyntaxList(location) &&
    1953            8 :                 isClassLike(location.parent)
    1954            8 :             )
    1955            8 :         );
    1956            8 : }
    1957            8 : 
    1958            8 : function getEntryForMemberCompletion(
    1959            8 :     host: LanguageServiceHost,
    1960            8 :     program: Program,
    1961            8 :     options: CompilerOptions,
    1962            8 :     preferences: UserPreferences,
    1963            8 :     name: string,
    1964            8 :     symbol: Symbol,
    1965            8 :     location: Node,
    1966            8 :     position: number,
    1967            8 :     contextToken: Node | undefined,
    1968            8 :     formatContext: formatting.FormatContext | undefined,
    1969            8 : ): { insertText: string; filterText?: string; isSnippet?: true; importAdder?: codefix.ImportAdder; eraseRange?: TextRange; } | undefined {
    1970            8 :     const classLikeDeclaration = findAncestor(location, isClassLike);
    1971            8 :     if (!classLikeDeclaration) {
    1972            8 :         return undefined; // This should never happen.
    1973            8 :     }
    1974            8 : 
    1975            8 :     let isSnippet: true | undefined;
    1976            8 :     let insertText: string = name;
    1977            8 :     const filterText: string = name;
    1978            8 : 
    1979            8 :     const checker = program.getTypeChecker();
    1980            8 :     const sourceFile = location.getSourceFile();
    1981            8 :     const printer = createSnippetPrinter({
    1982            8 :         removeComments: true,
    1983            8 :         module: options.module,
    1984            8 :         moduleResolution: options.moduleResolution,
    1985            8 :         target: options.target,
    1986            8 :         omitTrailingSemicolon: false,
    1987            8 :         newLine: getNewLineKind(getNewLineOrDefaultFromHost(host, formatContext?.options)),
    1988            8 :     });
    1989            8 :     const importAdder = codefix.createImportAdder(sourceFile, program, preferences, host);
    1990            8 : 
    1991            8 :     // Create empty body for possible method implementation.
    1992            8 :     let body;
    1993            8 :     if (preferences.includeCompletionsWithSnippetText) {
    1994            8 :         isSnippet = true;
    1995            8 :         // We are adding a tabstop (i.e. `$0`) in the body of the suggested member,
    1996            8 :         // if it has one, so that the cursor ends up in the body once the completion is inserted.
    1997            8 :         // Note: this assumes we won't have more than one body in the completion nodes, which should be the case.
    1998            8 :         const emptyStmt = factory.createEmptyStatement();
    1999            8 :         body = factory.createBlock([emptyStmt], /*multiLine*/ true);
    2000            8 :         setSnippetElement(emptyStmt, { kind: SnippetKind.TabStop, order: 0 });
    2001            8 :     }
    2002            8 :     else {
    2003            8 :         body = factory.createBlock([], /*multiLine*/ true);
    2004            8 :     }
    2005            8 : 
    2006            8 :     let modifiers = ModifierFlags.None;
    2007            8 :     const { modifiers: presentModifiers, range: eraseRange, decorators: presentDecorators } = getPresentModifiers(contextToken, sourceFile, position);
    2008            8 :     // Whether the suggested member should be abstract.
    2009            8 :     // e.g. in `abstract class C { abstract | }`, we should offer abstract method signatures at position `|`.
    2010            8 :     const isAbstract = presentModifiers & ModifierFlags.Abstract && classLikeDeclaration.modifierFlagsCache & ModifierFlags.Abstract;
    2011            8 :     let completionNodes: codefix.AddNode[] = [];
    2012            8 :     codefix.addNewNodeForMemberSymbol(
    2013            8 :         symbol,
    2014            8 :         classLikeDeclaration,
    2015            8 :         sourceFile,
    2016            8 :         { program, host },
    2017            8 :         preferences,
    2018            8 :         importAdder,
    2019            8 :         // `addNewNodeForMemberSymbol` calls this callback function for each new member node
    2020            8 :         // it adds for the given member symbol.
    2021            8 :         // We store these member nodes in the `completionNodes` array.
    2022            8 :         // Note: there might be:
    2023            8 :         //  - No nodes if `addNewNodeForMemberSymbol` cannot figure out a node for the member;
    2024            8 :         //  - One node;
    2025            8 :         //  - More than one node if the member is overloaded (e.g. a method with overload signatures).
    2026            8 :         node => {
    2027            8 :             let requiredModifiers = ModifierFlags.None;
    2028            8 :             if (isAbstract) {
    2029            8 :                 requiredModifiers |= ModifierFlags.Abstract;
    2030            8 :             }
    2031            8 :             if (
    2032            8 :                 isClassElement(node)
    2033            8 :                 && checker.getMemberOverrideModifierStatus(classLikeDeclaration, node, symbol) === MemberOverrideStatus.NeedsOverride
    2034            8 :             ) {
    2035            8 :                 requiredModifiers |= ModifierFlags.Override;
    2036            8 :             }
    2037            8 :             if (!completionNodes.length) {
    2038            8 :                 // Keep track of added missing required modifiers and modifiers already present.
    2039            8 :                 // This is needed when we have overloaded signatures,
    2040            8 :                 // so this callback will be called for multiple nodes/signatures,
    2041            8 :                 // and we need to make sure the modifiers are uniform for all nodes/signatures.
    2042            8 :                 modifiers = node.modifierFlagsCache | requiredModifiers;
    2043            8 :             }
    2044            8 :             node = factory.replaceModifiers(node, modifiers);
    2045            8 :             completionNodes.push(node);
    2046            8 :         },
    2047            8 :         body,
    2048            8 :         codefix.PreserveOptionalFlags.Property,
    2049            8 :         !!isAbstract,
    2050            8 :     );
    2051            8 : 
    2052            8 :     if (completionNodes.length) {
    2053            8 :         const isMethod = symbol.flags & SymbolFlags.Method;
    2054            8 :         let allowedModifiers = modifiers | ModifierFlags.Override | ModifierFlags.Public;
    2055            8 :         if (!isMethod) {
    2056            8 :             allowedModifiers |= ModifierFlags.Ambient | ModifierFlags.Readonly;
    2057            8 :         }
    2058            8 :         else {
    2059            8 :             allowedModifiers |= ModifierFlags.Async;
    2060            8 :         }
    2061            8 :         const allowedAndPresent = presentModifiers & allowedModifiers;
    2062            8 :         if (presentModifiers & (~allowedModifiers)) {
    2063            8 :             return undefined; // This completion entry will be filtered out.
    2064            8 :         }
    2065            8 :         // If the original member is protected, we allow it to change to public.
    2066            8 :         if (modifiers & ModifierFlags.Protected && allowedAndPresent & ModifierFlags.Public) {
    2067            8 :             modifiers &= ~ModifierFlags.Protected;
    2068            8 :         }
    2069            8 :         // `public` modifier is optional and can be dropped.
    2070            8 :         if (allowedAndPresent !== ModifierFlags.None && !(allowedAndPresent & ModifierFlags.Public)) {
    2071            8 :             modifiers &= ~ModifierFlags.Public;
    2072            8 :         }
    2073            8 :         modifiers |= allowedAndPresent;
    2074            8 :         completionNodes = completionNodes.map(node => factory.replaceModifiers(node, modifiers));
    2075            8 :         // Add back the decorators that were already present.
    2076            8 :         if (presentDecorators?.length) {
    2077            8 :             const lastNode = completionNodes[completionNodes.length - 1];
    2078            8 :             if (canHaveDecorators(lastNode)) {
    2079            8 :                 completionNodes[completionNodes.length - 1] = factory.replaceDecoratorsAndModifiers(lastNode, (presentDecorators as ModifierLike[]).concat(getModifiers(lastNode) || []));
    2080            8 :             }
    2081            8 :         }
    2082            8 : 
    2083            8 :         const format = ListFormat.MultiLine | ListFormat.NoTrailingNewLine;
    2084            8 :         // If we have access to formatting settings, we print the nodes using the emitter,
    2085            8 :         // and then format the printed text.
    2086            8 :         if (formatContext) {
    2087            8 :             insertText = printer.printAndFormatSnippetList(
    2088            8 :                 format,
    2089            8 :                 factory.createNodeArray(completionNodes),
    2090            8 :                 sourceFile,
    2091            8 :                 formatContext,
    2092            8 :             );
    2093            8 :         }
    2094            8 :         else { // Otherwise, just use emitter to print the new nodes.
    2095            8 :             insertText = printer.printSnippetList(
    2096            8 :                 format,
    2097            8 :                 factory.createNodeArray(completionNodes),
    2098            8 :                 sourceFile,
    2099            8 :             );
    2100            8 :         }
    2101            8 :     }
    2102            8 : 
    2103            8 :     return { insertText, filterText, isSnippet, importAdder, eraseRange };
    2104            8 : }
    2105            8 : 
    2106            8 : function getPresentModifiers(
    2107            8 :     contextToken: Node | undefined,
    2108            8 :     sourceFile: SourceFile,
    2109            8 :     position: number,
    2110            8 : ): { modifiers: ModifierFlags; decorators?: Decorator[]; range?: TextRange; } {
    2111            8 :     if (
    2112            8 :         !contextToken ||
    2113            8 :         getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(sourceFile, position).line
    2114            8 :             > getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(sourceFile, contextToken.getEnd()).line
    2115            8 :     ) {
    2116            8 :         return { modifiers: ModifierFlags.None };
    2117            8 :     }
    2118            8 :     let modifiers = ModifierFlags.None;
    2119            8 :     let decorators: Decorator[] | undefined;
    2120            8 :     let contextMod;
    2121            8 :     const range: TextRange = { pos: position, end: position };
    2122            8 : 
    2123            8 :     /*
    2124            8 :     Cases supported:
    2125            8 :     In
    2126            8 :     `class C {
    2127            8 :         public abstract |
    2128            8 :     }`
    2129            8 :     `contextToken` is ``abstract`` (as an identifier),
    2130            8 :     `contextToken.parent` is property declaration,
    2131            8 :     `location` is class declaration ``class C { ... }``.
    2132            8 :     In
    2133            8 :     `class C {
    2134            8 :         protected override m|
    2135            8 :     }`
    2136            8 :         `contextToken` is ``override`` (as a keyword),
    2137            8 :     `contextToken.parent` is property declaration,
    2138            8 :     `location` is identifier ``m``.
    2139            8 :     */
    2140            8 :     if (isPropertyDeclaration(contextToken.parent) && (contextMod = isModifierLike(contextToken))) {
    2141            8 :         if (contextToken.parent.modifiers) {
    2142            8 :             modifiers |= modifiersToFlags(contextToken.parent.modifiers) & ModifierFlags.Modifier;
    2143            8 :             decorators = contextToken.parent.modifiers.filter(isDecorator) || [];
    2144            8 :             range.pos = Math.min(...contextToken.parent.modifiers.map(n => n.getStart(sourceFile)));
    2145            8 :         }
    2146            8 :         const contextModifierFlag = modifierToFlag(contextMod);
    2147            8 :         if (!(modifiers & contextModifierFlag)) {
    2148            8 :             modifiers |= contextModifierFlag;
    2149            8 :             range.pos = Math.min(range.pos, contextToken.getStart(sourceFile));
    2150            8 :         }
    2151            8 :         /*
    2152            8 :         We have two cases:
    2153            8 :         1.
    2154            8 :         `class C {
    2155            8 :             modifier |
    2156            8 :         }`
    2157            8 :         `contextToken` is `modifier`,
    2158            8 :         and the range should be `modifier |`, ending at `position`,
    2159            8 :         and
    2160            8 :         2.
    2161            8 :         `class C {
    2162            8 :             modifier otherToken|
    2163            8 :         }`
    2164            8 :         `contextToken` is `modifier`,
    2165            8 :         `contextToken.parent.name` is `otherToken`,
    2166            8 :         and the range should be `modifier `, ending at the start of `otherToken`.
    2167            8 :         */
    2168            8 :         if (contextToken.parent.name !== contextToken) {
    2169            8 :             range.end = contextToken.parent.name.getStart(sourceFile);
    2170            8 :         }
    2171            8 :     }
    2172            8 :     return { modifiers, decorators, range: range.pos < range.end ? range : undefined };
    2173            8 : }
    2174            8 : 
    2175            8 : function isModifierLike(node: Node): ModifierSyntaxKind | undefined {
    2176            8 :     if (isModifier(node)) {
    2177            8 :         return node.kind;
    2178            8 :     }
    2179            8 :     if (isIdentifier(node)) {
    2180            8 :         const originalKeywordKind = identifierToKeywordKind(node);
    2181            8 :         if (originalKeywordKind && isModifierKind(originalKeywordKind)) {
    2182            8 :             return originalKeywordKind;
    2183            8 :         }
    2184            8 :     }
    2185            8 :     return undefined;
    2186            8 : }
    2187            8 : 
    2188            8 : function getEntryForObjectLiteralMethodCompletion(
    2189            8 :     symbol: Symbol,
    2190            8 :     name: string,
    2191            8 :     enclosingDeclaration: ObjectLiteralExpression,
    2192            8 :     program: Program,
    2193            8 :     host: LanguageServiceHost,

    2199            8 :     let insertText: string = name;
    2200            8 : 
    2201            8 :     const sourceFile = enclosingDeclaration.getSourceFile();
    2202            8 : 
    2203            8 :     const method = createObjectLiteralMethod(symbol, enclosingDeclaration, sourceFile, program, host, preferences);
    2204            8 :     if (!method) {
    2205            8 :         return undefined;
    2206            8 :     }

    2208            8 :     const printer = createSnippetPrinter({
    2209            8 :         removeComments: true,

    2215            8 :     });

    2218            8 :     }
    2219            8 :     else {
    2220            8 :         insertText = printer.printSnippetList(ListFormat.CommaDelimited | ListFormat.AllowTrailingComma, factory.createNodeArray([method], /*hasTrailingComma*/ true), sourceFile);
    2221            8 :     }
    2222            8 : 
    2223            8 :     const signaturePrinter = createPrinter({
    2224            8 :         removeComments: true,

    2227            8 :         target: options.target,
    2228            8 :         omitTrailingSemicolon: true,
    2229            8 :     });
    2230            8 :     // The `labelDetails.detail` will be displayed right beside the method name,
    2231            8 :     // so we drop the name (and modifiers) from the signature.
    2232            8 :     const methodSignature = factory.createMethodSignature(
    2233            8 :         /*modifiers*/ undefined,
    2234            8 :         /*name*/ "",
    2235            8 :         method.questionToken,
    2236            8 :         method.typeParameters,
    2237            8 :         method.parameters,
    2238            8 :         method.type,
    2239            8 :     );
    2240            8 :     const labelDetails = { detail: signaturePrinter.printNode(EmitHint.Unspecified, methodSignature, sourceFile) };
    2241            8 : 
    2242            8 :     return { isSnippet, insertText, labelDetails };
    2243            8 : }
    2244            8 : 
    2245            8 : function createObjectLiteralMethod(
    2246            8 :     symbol: Symbol,
    2247            8 :     enclosingDeclaration: ObjectLiteralExpression,
    2248            8 :     sourceFile: SourceFile,
    2249            8 :     program: Program,
    2250            8 :     host: LanguageServiceHost,
    2251            8 :     preferences: UserPreferences,
    2252            8 : ): MethodDeclaration | undefined {
    2253            8 :     const declarations = symbol.getDeclarations();
    2254            8 :     if (!(declarations && declarations.length)) {
    2255            8 :         return undefined;
    2256            8 :     }
    2257            8 :     const checker = program.getTypeChecker();
    2258            8 :     const declaration = declarations[0];
    2259            8 :     const name = getSynthesizedDeepClone(getNameOfDeclaration(declaration), /*includeTrivia*/ false) as PropertyName;
    2260            8 :     const type = checker.getWidenedType(checker.getTypeOfSymbolAtLocation(symbol, enclosingDeclaration));
    2261            8 :     const quotePreference = getQuotePreference(sourceFile, preferences);
    2262            8 :     const builderFlags = NodeBuilderFlags.OmitThisParameter | (quotePreference === QuotePreference.Single ? NodeBuilderFlags.UseSingleQuotesForStringLiteralType : NodeBuilderFlags.None);
    2263            8 : 
    2264            8 :     switch (declaration.kind) {
    2265            8 :         case SyntaxKind.PropertySignature:
    2266            8 :         case SyntaxKind.PropertyDeclaration:
    2267            8 :         case SyntaxKind.MethodSignature:
    2268            8 :         case SyntaxKind.MethodDeclaration: {
    2269            8 :             let effectiveType = type.flags & TypeFlags.Union && (type as UnionType).types.length < 10
    2270            8 :                 ? checker.getUnionType((type as UnionType).types, UnionReduction.Subtype)
    2271            8 :                 : type;
    2272            8 :             if (effectiveType.flags & TypeFlags.Union) {
    2273            8 :                 // Only offer the completion if there's a single function type component.
    2274            8 :                 const functionTypes = filter((effectiveType as UnionType).types, type => checker.getSignaturesOfType(type, SignatureKind.Call).length > 0);
    2275            8 :                 if (functionTypes.length === 1) {
    2276            8 :                     effectiveType = functionTypes[0];
    2277            8 :                 }
    2278            8 :                 else {
    2279            8 :                     return undefined;
    2280            8 :                 }
    2281            8 :             }
    2282            8 :             const signatures = checker.getSignaturesOfType(effectiveType, SignatureKind.Call);
    2283            8 :             if (signatures.length !== 1) {
    2284            8 :                 // We don't support overloads in object literals.
    2285            8 :                 return undefined;
    2286            8 :             }
    2287            8 :             const typeNode = checker.typeToTypeNode(effectiveType, enclosingDeclaration, builderFlags, codefix.getNoopSymbolTrackerWithResolver({ program, host }));
    2288            8 :             if (!typeNode || !isFunctionTypeNode(typeNode)) {
    2289            8 :                 return undefined;
    2290            8 :             }
    2291            8 : 
    2292            8 :             let body;
    2293            8 :             if (preferences.includeCompletionsWithSnippetText) {
    2294            8 :                 const emptyStmt = factory.createEmptyStatement();
    2295            8 :                 body = factory.createBlock([emptyStmt], /*multiLine*/ true);
    2296            8 :                 setSnippetElement(emptyStmt, { kind: SnippetKind.TabStop, order: 0 });
    2297            8 :             }
    2298            8 :             else {
    2299            8 :                 body = factory.createBlock([], /*multiLine*/ true);
    2300            8 :             }
    2301            8 : 
    2302            8 :             const parameters = typeNode.parameters.map(typedParam =>
    2303            8 :                 factory.createParameterDeclaration(
    2304            8 :                     /*modifiers*/ undefined,
    2305            8 :                     typedParam.dotDotDotToken,
    2306            8 :                     typedParam.name,
    2307            8 :                     /*questionToken*/ undefined,
    2308            8 :                     /*type*/ undefined,
    2309            8 :                     typedParam.initializer,
    2310            8 :                 )
    2311            8 :             );
    2312            8 :             return factory.createMethodDeclaration(
    2313            8 :                 /*modifiers*/ undefined,
    2314            8 :                 /*asteriskToken*/ undefined,
    2315            8 :                 name,
    2316            8 :                 /*questionToken*/ undefined,
    2317            8 :                 /*typeParameters*/ undefined,
    2318            8 :                 parameters,
    2319            8 :                 /*type*/ undefined,
    2320            8 :                 body,
    2321            8 :             );
    2322            8 :         }
    2323            8 :         default:
    2324            8 :             return undefined;
    2325            8 :     }
    2326            8 : }
    2327            8 : 
    2328            8 : function createSnippetPrinter(
    2329            8 :     printerOptions: PrinterOptions,
    2330            8 : ) {
    2331            8 :     let escapes: TextChange[] | undefined;
    2332            8 :     const baseWriter = textChanges.createWriter(getNewLineCharacter(printerOptions));
    2333            8 :     const printer = createPrinter(printerOptions, baseWriter);
    2334            8 :     const writer: EmitTextWriter = {
    2335            8 :         ...baseWriter,
    2336            8 :         write: s => escapingWrite(s, () => baseWriter.write(s)),
    2337            8 :         nonEscapingWrite: baseWriter.write,
    2338            8 :         writeLiteral: s => escapingWrite(s, () => baseWriter.writeLiteral(s)),
    2339            8 :         writeStringLiteral: s => escapingWrite(s, () => baseWriter.writeStringLiteral(s)),
    2340            8 :         writeSymbol: (s, symbol) => escapingWrite(s, () => baseWriter.writeSymbol(s, symbol)),
    2341            8 :         writeParameter: s => escapingWrite(s, () => baseWriter.writeParameter(s)),
    2342            8 :         writeComment: s => escapingWrite(s, () => baseWriter.writeComment(s)),
    2343            8 :         writeProperty: s => escapingWrite(s, () => baseWriter.writeProperty(s)),
    2344            8 :     };
    2345            8 : 
    2346            8 :     return {
    2347            8 :         printSnippetList,
    2348            8 :         printAndFormatSnippetList,
    2349            8 :         printNode,
    2350            8 :         printAndFormatNode,
    2351            8 :     };
    2352            8 : 
    2353            8 :     // The formatter/scanner will have issues with snippet-escaped text,
    2354            8 :     // so instead of writing the escaped text directly to the writer,
    2355            8 :     // generate a set of changes that can be applied to the unescaped text
    2356            8 :     // to escape it post-formatting.
    2357            8 :     function escapingWrite(s: string, write: () => void) {
    2358            8 :         const escaped = escapeSnippetText(s);
    2359            8 :         if (escaped !== s) {
    2360            8 :             const start = baseWriter.getTextPos();
    2361            8 :             write();
    2362            8 :             const end = baseWriter.getTextPos();
    2363            8 :             escapes = append(escapes ||= [], { newText: escaped, span: { start, length: end - start } });
    2364            8 :         }
    2365            8 :         else {
    2366            8 :             write();
    2367            8 :         }
    2368            8 :     }
    2369            8 : 
    2370            8 :     /** Snippet-escaping version of `printer.printList`. */
    2371            8 :     function printSnippetList(
    2372            8 :         format: ListFormat,
    2373            8 :         list: NodeArray<Node>,
    2374            8 :         sourceFile: SourceFile | undefined,
    2375            8 :     ): string {
    2376            8 :         const unescaped = printUnescapedSnippetList(format, list, sourceFile);
    2377            8 :         return escapes ? textChanges.applyChanges(unescaped, escapes) : unescaped;
    2378            8 :     }
    2379            8 : 
    2380            8 :     function printUnescapedSnippetList(
    2381            8 :         format: ListFormat,
    2382            8 :         list: NodeArray<Node>,
    2383            8 :         sourceFile: SourceFile | undefined,
    2384            8 :     ): string {
    2385            8 :         escapes = undefined;
    2386            8 :         writer.clear();
    2387            8 :         printer.writeList(format, list, sourceFile, writer);
    2388            8 :         return writer.getText();
    2389            8 :     }
    2390            8 : 
    2391            8 :     function printAndFormatSnippetList(
    2392            8 :         format: ListFormat,
    2393            8 :         list: NodeArray<Node>,
    2394            8 :         sourceFile: SourceFile,
    2395            8 :         formatContext: formatting.FormatContext,
    2396            8 :     ): string {
    2397            8 :         const syntheticFile = {
    2398            8 :             text: printUnescapedSnippetList(
    2399            8 :                 format,
    2400            8 :                 list,
    2401            8 :                 sourceFile,
    2402            8 :             ),
    2403            8 :             getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(pos: number) {
    2404            8 :                 return getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(this, pos);
    2405            8 :             },
    2406            8 :         };
    2407            8 : 
    2408            8 :         const formatOptions = getFormatCodeSettingsForWriting(formatContext, sourceFile);
    2409            8 :         const changes = flatMap(list, node => {
    2410            8 :             const nodeWithPos = textChanges.assignPositionsToNode(node);
    2411            8 :             return formatting.formatNodeGivenIndentation(
    2412            8 :                 nodeWithPos,
    2413            8 :                 syntheticFile,
    2414            8 :                 sourceFile.languageVariant,
    2415            8 :                 /* indentation */ 0,
    2416            8 :                 /* delta */ 0,
    2417            8 :                 { ...formatContext, options: formatOptions },
    2418            8 :             );
    2419            8 :         });
    2420            8 : 
    2421            8 :         const allChanges = escapes
    2422            8 :             ? stableSort(concatenate(changes, escapes), (a, b) => compareTextSpans(a.span, b.span))
    2423            8 :             : changes;
    2424            8 :         return textChanges.applyChanges(syntheticFile.text, allChanges);
    2425            8 :     }
    2426            8 : 
    2427            8 :     /** Snippet-escaping version of `printer.printNode`. */
    2428            8 :     function printNode(hint: EmitHint, node: Node, sourceFile: SourceFile): string {
    2429            8 :         const unescaped = printUnescapedNode(hint, node, sourceFile);
    2430            8 :         return escapes ? textChanges.applyChanges(unescaped, escapes) : unescaped;
    2431            8 :     }
    2432            8 : 
    2433            8 :     function printUnescapedNode(hint: EmitHint, node: Node, sourceFile: SourceFile): string {
    2434            8 :         escapes = undefined;
    2435            8 :         writer.clear();
    2436            8 :         printer.writeNode(hint, node, sourceFile, writer);
    2437            8 :         return writer.getText();
    2438            8 :     }
    2439            8 : 
    2440            8 :     function printAndFormatNode(
    2441            8 :         hint: EmitHint,
    2442            8 :         node: Node,
    2443            8 :         sourceFile: SourceFile,
    2444            8 :         formatContext: formatting.FormatContext,
    2445            8 :     ): string {
    2446            8 :         const syntheticFile = {
    2447            8 :             text: printUnescapedNode(
    2448            8 :                 hint,
    2449            8 :                 node,
    2450            8 :                 sourceFile,
    2451            8 :             ),
    2452            8 :             getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(pos: number) {
    2453            8 :                 return getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(this, pos);
    2454            8 :             },
    2455            8 :         };
    2456            8 : 
    2457            8 :         const formatOptions = getFormatCodeSettingsForWriting(formatContext, sourceFile);
    2458            8 :         const nodeWithPos = textChanges.assignPositionsToNode(node);
    2459            8 :         const changes = formatting.formatNodeGivenIndentation(
    2460            8 :             nodeWithPos,
    2461            8 :             syntheticFile,
    2462            8 :             sourceFile.languageVariant,
    2463            8 :             /* indentation */ 0,
    2464            8 :             /* delta */ 0,
    2465            8 :             { ...formatContext, options: formatOptions },
    2466            8 :         );
    2467            8 : 
    2468            8 :         const allChanges = escapes
    2469            8 :             ? stableSort(concatenate(changes, escapes), (a, b) => compareTextSpans(a.span, b.span))
    2470            8 :             : changes;
    2471            8 :         return textChanges.applyChanges(syntheticFile.text, allChanges);
    2472            8 :     }
    2473            8 : }
    2474            8 : 
    2475            8 : function originToCompletionEntryData(origin: SymbolOriginInfoExport | SymbolOriginInfoResolvedExport): CompletionEntryData | undefined {
    2476            8 :     const ambientModuleName = origin.fileName ? undefined : stripQuotes(origin.moduleSymbol.name);
    2477            8 :     const isPackageJsonImport = origin.isFromPackageJson ? true : undefined;

    2681            8 :     function shouldIncludeSymbol(symbol: Symbol, symbolToSortTextMap: SymbolSortTextMap): boolean {
    2682            8 :         let allFlags = symbol.flags;
    2683            8 :         if (!isSourceFile(location)) {
    2684            8 :             // export = /**/ here we want to get all meanings, so any symbol is ok
    2685            8 :             if (isExportAssignment(location.parent)) {
    2686            8 :                 return true;
    2687            8 :             }
    2688            8 :             // Filter out variables from their own initializers
    2689            8 :             // `const a = /* no 'a' here */`
    2690            8 :             if (tryCast(variableOrParameterDeclaration, isVariableDeclaration) && symbol.valueDeclaration === variableOrParameterDeclaration) {
    2691            8 :                 return false;
    2692            8 :             }
    2693            8 : 
    2694            8 :             // Filter out parameters from their own initializers
    2695            8 :             // `function f(a = /* no 'a' and 'b' here */, b) { }` or
    2696            8 :             // `function f<T = /* no 'T' here */>(a: T) { }`
    2697            8 :             const symbolDeclaration = symbol.valueDeclaration ?? symbol.declarations?.[0];
    2698            8 :             if (
    2699            8 :                 variableOrParameterDeclaration && symbolDeclaration && (
    2700            8 :                     (isTypeParameterDeclaration(variableOrParameterDeclaration) && isTypeParameterDeclaration(symbolDeclaration)) ||
    2701            8 :                     (isParameter(variableOrParameterDeclaration) && isParameter(symbolDeclaration))
    2702            8 :                 )
    2703            8 :             ) {
    2704            8 :                 const symbolDeclarationPos = symbolDeclaration.pos;
    2705            8 :                 const parameters = isParameter(variableOrParameterDeclaration) ? variableOrParameterDeclaration.parent.parameters :
    2706            8 :                     isInferTypeNode(variableOrParameterDeclaration.parent) ? undefined :
    2707            8 :                     variableOrParameterDeclaration.parent.typeParameters;
    2708            8 :                 if (symbolDeclarationPos >= variableOrParameterDeclaration.pos && parameters && symbolDeclarationPos < parameters.end) {
    2709            8 :                     return false;
    2710            8 :                 }
    2711            8 :             }
    2712            8 : 
    2713            8 :             // External modules can have global export declarations that will be
    2714            8 :             // available as global keywords in all scopes. But if the external module
    2715            8 :             // already has an explicit export and user only wants to user explicit
    2716            8 :             // module imports then the global keywords will be filtered out so auto
    2717            8 :             // import suggestions will win in the completion
    2718            8 :             const symbolOrigin = skipAlias(symbol, typeChecker);
    2719            8 :             // We only want to filter out the global keywords
    2720            8 :             // Auto Imports are not available for scripts so this conditional is always false
    2721            8 :             if (
    2722            8 :                 !!sourceFile.externalModuleIndicator
    2723            8 :                 && !compilerOptions.allowUmdGlobalAccess
    2724            8 :                 && symbolToSortTextMap[getSymbolId(symbol)] === SortText.GlobalsOrKeywords
    2725            8 :                 && (symbolToSortTextMap[getSymbolId(symbolOrigin)] === SortText.AutoImportSuggestions
    2726            8 :                     || symbolToSortTextMap[getSymbolId(symbolOrigin)] === SortText.LocationPriority)
    2727            8 :             ) {
    2728            8 :                 return false;
    2729            8 :             }
    2730            8 : 
    2731            8 :             allFlags |= getCombinedLocalAndExportSymbolFlags(symbolOrigin);
    2732            8 : 
    2733            8 :             // import m = /**/ <-- It can only access namespace (if typing import = x. this would get member symbols and not namespace)
    2734            8 :             if (isInRightSideOfInternalImportEqualsDeclaration(location)) {
    2735            8 :                 return !!(allFlags & SymbolFlags.Namespace);
    2736            8 :             }
    2737            8 : 
    2738            8 :             if (isTypeOnlyLocation) {
    2739            8 :                 // It's a type, but you can reach it by namespace.type as well
    2740            8 :                 return symbolCanBeReferencedAtTypeLocation(symbol, typeChecker);
    2741            8 :             }
    2742            8 :         }
    2743            8 : 
    2744            8 :         // expressions are value space (which includes the value namespaces)
    2745            8 :         return !!(allFlags & SymbolFlags.Value);
    2746            8 :     }
    2747            8 : 
    2748            8 :     function symbolAppearsToBeTypeOnly(symbol: Symbol): boolean {

    2750            8 :         return !(flags & SymbolFlags.Value) && (!isInJSFile(symbol.declarations?.[0]) || !!(flags & SymbolFlags.Type));

    2761            8 : function getLabelStatementCompletions(node: Node): CompletionEntry[] {

    2909            8 :         }

    3178            8 : function getContextualType(previousToken: Node, position: number, sourceFile: SourceFile, checker: TypeChecker): Type | undefined {
    3179            8 :     const { parent } = previousToken;
    3180            8 :     switch (previousToken.kind) {
    3181            8 :         case SyntaxKind.Identifier:
    3182            8 :             return getContextualTypeFromParent(previousToken as Identifier, checker);
    3183            8 :         case SyntaxKind.EqualsToken:
    3184            8 :             switch (parent.kind) {
    3185            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.VariableDeclaration:
    3186            8 :                     return checker.getContextualType((parent as VariableDeclaration).initializer!); // TODO: GH#18217
    3187            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.BinaryExpression:
    3188            8 :                     return checker.getTypeAtLocation((parent as BinaryExpression).left);
    3189            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxAttribute:
    3190            8 :                     return checker.getContextualTypeForJsxAttribute(parent as JsxAttribute);
    3191            8 :                 default:
    3192            8 :                     return undefined;
    3193            8 :             }
    3194            8 :         case SyntaxKind.NewKeyword:
    3195            8 :             return checker.getContextualType(parent as Expression);
    3196            8 :         case SyntaxKind.CaseKeyword:
    3197            8 :             const caseClause = tryCast(parent, isCaseClause);
    3198            8 :             return caseClause ? getSwitchedType(caseClause, checker) : undefined;
    3199            8 :         case SyntaxKind.OpenBraceToken:
    3200            8 :             return isJsxExpression(parent) && !isJsxElement(parent.parent) && !isJsxFragment(parent.parent) ? checker.getContextualTypeForJsxAttribute(parent.parent) : undefined;
    3201            8 :         default:
    3202            8 :             const argInfo = SignatureHelp.getArgumentInfoForCompletions(previousToken, position, sourceFile, checker);
    3203            8 :             return argInfo ?
    3204            8 :                 checker.getContextualTypeForArgumentAtIndex(argInfo.invocation, argInfo.argumentIndex) :
    3205            8 :                 isEqualityOperatorKind(previousToken.kind) && isBinaryExpression(parent) && isEqualityOperatorKind(parent.operatorToken.kind) ?
    3206            8 :                 // completion at `x ===/**/` should be for the right side

    3361            8 :             // to opt in with the `includeCompletionsForImportStatements` user preference.
    3362            8 :             flags |= CompletionInfoFlags.IsImportStatementCompletion;
    3363            8 :             importStatementCompletion = importStatementCompletionInfo;
    3364            8 :             isNewIdentifierLocation = importStatementCompletionInfo.isNewIdentifierLocation;
    3365            8 :         }
    3366            8 :         // Bail out if this is a known invalid completion location
    3367            8 :         if (!importStatementCompletionInfo.replacementSpan && isCompletionListBlocker(contextToken)) {
    3368            8 :             log("Returning an empty list because completion was requested in an invalid position.");
    3369            8 :             return keywordFilters
    3370            8 :                 ? keywordCompletionData(keywordFilters, isJsOnlyLocation, isNewIdentifierDefinitionLocation())
    3371            8 :                 : undefined;
    3372            8 :         }
    3373            8 : 
    3374            8 :         let parent = contextToken.parent;
    3375            8 :         if (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.DotToken || contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.QuestionDotToken) {
    3376            8 :             isRightOfDot = contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.DotToken;
    3377            8 :             isRightOfQuestionDot = contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.QuestionDotToken;
    3378            8 :             switch (parent.kind) {
    3379            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PropertyAccessExpression:
    3380            8 :                     propertyAccessToConvert = parent as PropertyAccessExpression;
    3381            8 :                     node = propertyAccessToConvert.expression;
    3382            8 :                     const leftmostAccessExpression = getLeftmostAccessExpression(propertyAccessToConvert);
    3383            8 :                     if (
    3384            8 :                         nodeIsMissing(leftmostAccessExpression) ||
    3385            8 :                         ((isCallExpression(node) || isFunctionLike(node)) &&
    3386            8 :                             node.end === contextToken.pos &&
    3387            8 :                             node.getChildCount(sourceFile) &&
    3388            8 :                             last(node.getChildren(sourceFile)).kind !== SyntaxKind.CloseParenToken)
    3389            8 :                     ) {
    3390            8 :                         // This is likely dot from incorrectly parsed expression and user is starting to write spread
    3391            8 :                         // eg: Math.min(./**/)
    3392            8 :                         // const x = function (./**/) {}
    3393            8 :                         // ({./**/})
    3394            8 :                         return undefined;
    3395            8 :                     }
    3396            8 :                     break;
    3397            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.QualifiedName:
    3398            8 :                     node = (parent as QualifiedName).left;
    3399            8 :                     break;
    3400            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ModuleDeclaration:
    3401            8 :                     node = (parent as ModuleDeclaration).name;
    3402            8 :                     break;
    3403            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ImportType:
    3404            8 :                     node = parent;
    3405            8 :                     break;
    3406            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.MetaProperty:
    3407            8 :                     node = parent.getFirstToken(sourceFile)!;
    3408            8 :                     Debug.assert(node.kind === SyntaxKind.ImportKeyword || node.kind === SyntaxKind.NewKeyword);
    3409            8 :                     break;
    3410            8 :                 default:
    3411            8 :                     // There is nothing that precedes the dot, so this likely just a stray character
    3412            8 :                     // or leading into a '...' token. Just bail out instead.
    3413            8 :                     return undefined;
    3414            8 :             }
    3415            8 :         }
    3416            8 :         else if (!importStatementCompletion) {
    3417            8 :             // <UI.Test /* completion position */ />
    3418            8 :             // If the tagname is a property access expression, we will then walk up to the top most of property access expression.
    3419            8 :             // Then, try to get a JSX container and its associated attributes type.
    3420            8 :             if (parent && parent.kind === SyntaxKind.PropertyAccessExpression) {
    3421            8 :                 contextToken = parent;
    3422            8 :                 parent = parent.parent;
    3423            8 :             }
    3424            8 : 
    3425            8 :             // Fix location
    3426            8 :             if (currentToken.parent === location) {
    3427            8 :                 switch (currentToken.kind) {
    3428            8 :                     case SyntaxKind.GreaterThanToken:
    3429            8 :                         if (currentToken.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxElement || currentToken.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxOpeningElement) {
    3430            8 :                             location = currentToken;
    3431            8 :                         }
    3432            8 :                         break;
    3433            8 : 
    3434            8 :                     case SyntaxKind.SlashToken:
    3435            8 :                         if (currentToken.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxSelfClosingElement) {
    3436            8 :                             location = currentToken;
    3437            8 :                         }
    3438            8 :                         break;
    3439            8 :                 }
    3440            8 :             }
    3441            8 : 
    3442            8 :             switch (parent.kind) {
    3443            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxClosingElement:
    3444            8 :                     if (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.SlashToken) {
    3445            8 :                         isStartingCloseTag = true;
    3446            8 :                         location = contextToken;
    3447            8 :                     }
    3448            8 :                     break;
    3449            8 : 
    3450            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.BinaryExpression:
    3451            8 :                     if (!binaryExpressionMayBeOpenTag(parent as BinaryExpression)) {
    3452            8 :                         break;
    3453            8 :                     }
    3454            8 :                 // falls through
    3455            8 : 
    3456            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxSelfClosingElement:
    3457            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxElement:
    3458            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxOpeningElement:
    3459            8 :                     isJsxIdentifierExpected = true;
    3460            8 :                     if (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.LessThanToken) {
    3461            8 :                         isRightOfOpenTag = true;
    3462            8 :                         location = contextToken;
    3463            8 :                     }
    3464            8 :                     break;
    3465            8 : 
    3466            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxExpression:
    3467            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxSpreadAttribute:
    3468            8 :                     // First case is for `<div foo={true} [||] />` or `<div foo={true} [||] ></div>`,
    3469            8 :                     // `parent` will be `{true}` and `previousToken` will be `}`
    3470            8 :                     // Second case is for `<div foo={true} t[||] ></div>`
    3471            8 :                     // Second case must not match for `<div foo={undefine[||]}></div>`
    3472            8 :                     if (previousToken.kind === SyntaxKind.CloseBraceToken || (previousToken.kind === SyntaxKind.Identifier && previousToken.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxAttribute)) {
    3473            8 :                         isJsxIdentifierExpected = true;
    3474            8 :                     }
    3475            8 :                     break;
    3476            8 : 
    3477            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxAttribute:
    3478            8 :                     // For `<div className="x" [||] ></div>`, `parent` will be JsxAttribute and `previousToken` will be its initializer
    3479            8 :                     if (
    3480            8 :                         (parent as JsxAttribute).initializer === previousToken &&
    3481            8 :                         previousToken.end < position
    3482            8 :                     ) {
    3483            8 :                         isJsxIdentifierExpected = true;
    3484            8 :                         break;
    3485            8 :                     }
    3486            8 :                     switch (previousToken.kind) {
    3487            8 :                         case SyntaxKind.EqualsToken:
    3488            8 :                             isJsxInitializer = true;
    3489            8 :                             break;
    3490            8 :                         case SyntaxKind.Identifier:
    3491            8 :                             isJsxIdentifierExpected = true;
    3492            8 :                             // For `<div x=[|f/**/|]`, `parent` will be `x` and `previousToken.parent` will be `f` (which is its own JsxAttribute)
    3493            8 :                             // Note for `<div someBool f>` we don't want to treat this as a jsx inializer, instead it's the attribute name.
    3494            8 :                             if (
    3495            8 :                                 parent !== previousToken.parent &&
    3496            8 :                                 !(parent as JsxAttribute).initializer &&
    3497            8 :                                 findChildOfKind(parent, SyntaxKind.EqualsToken, sourceFile)
    3498            8 :                             ) {
    3499            8 :                                 isJsxInitializer = previousToken as Identifier;
    3500            8 :                             }
    3501            8 :                     }
    3502            8 :                     break;
    3503            8 :             }
    3504            8 :         }
    3505            8 :     }
    3506            8 : 
    3507            8 :     const semanticStart = timestamp();
    3508            8 :     let completionKind = CompletionKind.None;
    3509            8 :     let hasUnresolvedAutoImports = false;
    3510            8 :     // This also gets mutated in nested-functions after the return
    3511            8 :     let symbols: Symbol[] = [];
    3512            8 :     let importSpecifierResolver: codefix.ImportSpecifierResolver | undefined;
    3513            8 :     const symbolToOriginInfoMap: SymbolOriginInfoMap = [];
    3514            8 :     const symbolToSortTextMap: SymbolSortTextMap = [];
    3515            8 :     const seenPropertySymbols = new Map<SymbolId, true>();
    3516            8 :     const isTypeOnlyLocation = isTypeOnlyCompletion();
    3517            8 :     const getModuleSpecifierResolutionHost = memoizeOne((isFromPackageJson: boolean) => {
    3518            8 :         return createModuleSpecifierResolutionHost(isFromPackageJson ? host.getPackageJsonAutoImportProvider!()! : program, host);
    3519            8 :     });
    3520            8 : 
    3521            8 :     if (isRightOfDot || isRightOfQuestionDot) {
    3522            8 :         getTypeScriptMemberSymbols();
    3523            8 :     }
    3524            8 :     else if (isRightOfOpenTag) {
    3525            8 :         symbols = typeChecker.getJsxIntrinsicTagNamesAt(location);
    3526            8 :         Debug.assertEachIsDefined(symbols, "getJsxIntrinsicTagNames() should all be defined");
    3527            8 :         tryGetGlobalSymbols();
    3528            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.Global;
    3529            8 :         keywordFilters = KeywordCompletionFilters.None;
    3530            8 :     }
    3531            8 :     else if (isStartingCloseTag) {
    3532            8 :         const tagName = (contextToken.parent.parent as JsxElement).openingElement.tagName;
    3533            8 :         const tagSymbol = typeChecker.getSymbolAtLocation(tagName);
    3534            8 :         if (tagSymbol) {
    3535            8 :             symbols = [tagSymbol];
    3536            8 :         }
    3537            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.Global;
    3538            8 :         keywordFilters = KeywordCompletionFilters.None;
    3539            8 :     }
    3540            8 :     else {
    3541            8 :         // For JavaScript or TypeScript, if we're not after a dot, then just try to get the
    3542            8 :         // global symbols in scope.  These results should be valid for either language as
    3543            8 :         // the set of symbols that can be referenced from this location.
    3544            8 :         if (!tryGetGlobalSymbols()) {
    3545            8 :             return keywordFilters
    3546            8 :                 ? keywordCompletionData(keywordFilters, isJsOnlyLocation, isNewIdentifierLocation)
    3547            8 :                 : undefined;
    3548            8 :         }
    3549            8 :     }
    3550            8 : 
    3551            8 :     log("getCompletionData: Semantic work: " + (timestamp() - semanticStart));
    3552            8 :     const contextualType = previousToken && getContextualType(previousToken, position, sourceFile, typeChecker);
    3553            8 : 
    3554            8 :     // exclude literal suggestions after <input type="text" [||] /> (#51667) and after closing quote (#52675)
    3555            8 :     // for strings getStringLiteralCompletions handles completions
    3556            8 :     const isLiteralExpected = !tryCast(previousToken, isStringLiteralLike) && !isJsxIdentifierExpected;
    3557            8 :     const literals = !isLiteralExpected ? [] : mapDefined(
    3558            8 :         contextualType && (contextualType.isUnion() ? contextualType.types : [contextualType]),
    3559            8 :         t => t.isLiteral() && !(t.flags & TypeFlags.EnumLiteral) ? t.value : undefined,
    3560            8 :     );
    3561            8 : 
    3562            8 :     const recommendedCompletion = previousToken && contextualType && getRecommendedCompletion(previousToken, contextualType, typeChecker);
    3563            8 :     return {
    3564            8 :         kind: CompletionDataKind.Data,
    3565            8 :         symbols,
    3566            8 :         completionKind,
    3567            8 :         isInSnippetScope,
    3568            8 :         propertyAccessToConvert,
    3569            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation,
    3570            8 :         location,
    3571            8 :         keywordFilters,
    3572            8 :         literals,

    3588            8 : 
    3589            8 :     type JSDocTagWithTypeExpression =
    3590            8 :         | JSDocParameterTag
    3591            8 :         | JSDocPropertyTag
    3592            8 :         | JSDocReturnTag
    3593            8 :         | JSDocTypeTag
    3594            8 :         | JSDocTypedefTag
    3595            8 :         | JSDocTemplateTag
    3596            8 :         | JSDocThrowsTag
    3597            8 :         | JSDocSatisfiesTag;
    3598            8 : 
    3599            8 :     function isTagWithTypeExpression(tag: JSDocTag): tag is JSDocTagWithTypeExpression {
    3600            8 :         switch (tag.kind) {
    3601            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JSDocParameterTag:
    3602            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JSDocPropertyTag:
    3603            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JSDocReturnTag:
    3604            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JSDocTypeTag:
    3605            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JSDocTypedefTag:
    3606            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JSDocThrowsTag:
    3607            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JSDocSatisfiesTag:
    3608            8 :                 return true;
    3609            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JSDocTemplateTag:
    3610            8 :                 return !!(tag as JSDocTemplateTag).constraint;
    3611            8 :             default:
    3612            8 :                 return false;
    3613            8 :         }
    3614            8 :     }
    3615            8 : 
    3616            8 :     function tryGetTypeExpressionFromTag(tag: JSDocTag): JSDocTypeExpression | ExpressionWithTypeArguments | undefined {
    3617            8 :         if (isTagWithTypeExpression(tag)) {
    3618            8 :             const typeExpression = isJSDocTemplateTag(tag) ? tag.constraint : tag.typeExpression;
    3619            8 :             return typeExpression && typeExpression.kind === SyntaxKind.JSDocTypeExpression ? typeExpression : undefined;
    3620            8 :         }
    3621            8 :         if (isJSDocAugmentsTag(tag) || isJSDocImplementsTag(tag)) {
    3622            8 :             return tag.class;
    3623            8 :         }
    3624            8 :         return undefined;
    3625            8 :     }
    3626            8 : 
    3627            8 :     function getTypeScriptMemberSymbols(): void {
    3628            8 :         // Right of dot member completion list
    3629            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.PropertyAccess;
    3630            8 : 
    3631            8 :         // Since this is qualified name check it's a type node location
    3632            8 :         const isImportType = isLiteralImportTypeNode(node);
    3633            8 :         const isTypeLocation = (isImportType && !(node as ImportTypeNode).isTypeOf)
    3634            8 :             || isPartOfTypeNode(node.parent)
    3635            8 :             || isPossiblyTypeArgumentPosition(contextToken, sourceFile, typeChecker);
    3636            8 :         const isRhsOfImportDeclaration = isInRightSideOfInternalImportEqualsDeclaration(node);
    3637            8 :         if (isEntityName(node) || isImportType || isPropertyAccessExpression(node)) {
    3638            8 :             const isNamespaceName = isModuleDeclaration(node.parent);
    3639            8 :             if (isNamespaceName) isNewIdentifierLocation = true;
    3640            8 :             let symbol = typeChecker.getSymbolAtLocation(node);
    3641            8 :             if (symbol) {
    3642            8 :                 symbol = skipAlias(symbol, typeChecker);
    3643            8 :                 if (symbol.flags & (SymbolFlags.Module | SymbolFlags.Enum)) {
    3644            8 :                     // Extract module or enum members
    3645            8 :                     const exportedSymbols = typeChecker.getExportsOfModule(symbol);
    3646            8 :                     Debug.assertEachIsDefined(exportedSymbols, "getExportsOfModule() should all be defined");
    3647            8 :                     const isValidValueAccess = (symbol: Symbol) => typeChecker.isValidPropertyAccess(isImportType ? node as ImportTypeNode : (node.parent as PropertyAccessExpression), symbol.name);
    3648            8 :                     const isValidTypeAccess = (symbol: Symbol) => symbolCanBeReferencedAtTypeLocation(symbol, typeChecker);
    3649            8 :                     const isValidAccess: (symbol: Symbol) => boolean = isNamespaceName
    3650            8 :                         // At `namespace N.M/**/`, if this is the only declaration of `M`, don't include `M` as a completion.
    3651            8 :                         ? symbol => !!(symbol.flags & SymbolFlags.Namespace) && !symbol.declarations?.every(d => d.parent === node.parent)
    3652            8 :                         : isRhsOfImportDeclaration ?
    3653            8 :                         // Any kind is allowed when dotting off namespace in internal import equals declaration
    3654            8 :                         symbol => isValidTypeAccess(symbol) || isValidValueAccess(symbol) :
    3655            8 :                         isTypeLocation || insideJsDocTagTypeExpression ? isValidTypeAccess : isValidValueAccess;
    3656            8 :                     for (const exportedSymbol of exportedSymbols) {
    3657            8 :                         if (isValidAccess(exportedSymbol)) {
    3658            8 :                             symbols.push(exportedSymbol);
    3659            8 :                         }
    3660            8 :                     }
    3661            8 : 
    3662            8 :                     // If the module is merged with a value, we must get the type of the class and add its propertes (for inherited static methods).
    3663            8 :                     if (
    3664            8 :                         !isTypeLocation &&
    3665            8 :                         !insideJsDocTagTypeExpression &&
    3666            8 :                         symbol.declarations &&
    3667            8 :                         symbol.declarations.some(d => d.kind !== SyntaxKind.SourceFile && d.kind !== SyntaxKind.ModuleDeclaration && d.kind !== SyntaxKind.EnumDeclaration)
    3668            8 :                     ) {
    3669            8 :                         let type = typeChecker.getTypeOfSymbolAtLocation(symbol, node).getNonOptionalType();
    3670            8 :                         let insertQuestionDot = false;
    3671            8 :                         if (type.isNullableType()) {
    3672            8 :                             const canCorrectToQuestionDot = isRightOfDot &&
    3673            8 :                                 !isRightOfQuestionDot &&
    3674            8 :                                 preferences.includeAutomaticOptionalChainCompletions !== false;
    3675            8 : 
    3676            8 :                             if (canCorrectToQuestionDot || isRightOfQuestionDot) {
    3677            8 :                                 type = type.getNonNullableType();
    3678            8 :                                 if (canCorrectToQuestionDot) {
    3679            8 :                                     insertQuestionDot = true;
    3680            8 :                                 }
    3681            8 :                             }
    3682            8 :                         }
    3683            8 :                         addTypeProperties(type, !!(node.flags & NodeFlags.AwaitContext), insertQuestionDot);
    3684            8 :                     }
    3685            8 : 
    3686            8 :                     return;
    3687            8 :                 }
    3688            8 :             }
    3689            8 :         }
    3690            8 : 
    3691            8 :         if (!isTypeLocation || isInTypeQuery(node)) {
    3692            8 :             // GH#39946. Pulling on the type of a node inside of a function with a contextual `this` parameter can result in a circularity
    3693            8 :             // if the `node` is part of the exprssion of a `yield` or `return`. This circularity doesn't exist at compile time because
    3694            8 :             // we will check (and cache) the type of `this` *before* checking the type of the node.
    3695            8 :             typeChecker.tryGetThisTypeAt(node, /*includeGlobalThis*/ false);

    3697            8 : 
    3698            8 :             if (!isTypeLocation) {
    3699            8 :                 let insertQuestionDot = false;
    3700            8 :                 if (type.isNullableType()) {
    3701            8 :                     const canCorrectToQuestionDot = isRightOfDot &&
    3702            8 :                         !isRightOfQuestionDot &&
    3703            8 :                         preferences.includeAutomaticOptionalChainCompletions !== false;
    3704            8 : 
    3705            8 :                     if (canCorrectToQuestionDot || isRightOfQuestionDot) {
    3706            8 :                         type = type.getNonNullableType();
    3707            8 :                         if (canCorrectToQuestionDot) {
    3708            8 :                             insertQuestionDot = true;
    3709            8 :                         }
    3710            8 :                     }
    3711            8 :                 }
    3712            8 :                 addTypeProperties(type, !!(node.flags & NodeFlags.AwaitContext), insertQuestionDot);
    3713            8 :             }
    3714            8 :             else {
    3715            8 :                 addTypeProperties(type.getNonNullableType(), /*insertAwait*/ false, /*insertQuestionDot*/ false);
    3716            8 :             }
    3717            8 :         }
    3718            8 :     }
    3719            8 : 
    3720            8 :     function addTypeProperties(type: Type, insertAwait: boolean, insertQuestionDot: boolean): void {
    3721            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation = !!type.getStringIndexType();
    3722            8 :         if (isRightOfQuestionDot && some(type.getCallSignatures())) {
    3723            8 :             isNewIdentifierLocation = true;
    3724            8 :         }
    3725            8 : 
    3726            8 :         const propertyAccess = node.kind === SyntaxKind.ImportType ? node as ImportTypeNode : node.parent as PropertyAccessExpression | QualifiedName;
    3727            8 :         if (inCheckedFile) {
    3728            8 :             for (const symbol of type.getApparentProperties()) {
    3729            8 :                 if (typeChecker.isValidPropertyAccessForCompletions(propertyAccess, type, symbol)) {
    3730            8 :                     addPropertySymbol(symbol, /*insertAwait*/ false, insertQuestionDot);
    3731            8 :                 }
    3732            8 :             }
    3733            8 :         }
    3734            8 :         else {
    3735            8 :             // In javascript files, for union types, we don't just get the members that
    3736            8 :             // the individual types have in common, we also include all the members that
    3737            8 :             // each individual type has. This is because we're going to add all identifiers
    3738            8 :             // anyways. So we might as well elevate the members that were at least part
    3739            8 :             // of the individual types to a higher status since we know what they are.
    3740            8 :             symbols.push(...filter(getPropertiesForCompletion(type, typeChecker), s => typeChecker.isValidPropertyAccessForCompletions(propertyAccess, type, s)));
    3741            8 :         }
    3742            8 : 
    3743            8 :         if (insertAwait && preferences.includeCompletionsWithInsertText) {
    3744            8 :             const promiseType = typeChecker.getPromisedTypeOfPromise(type);
    3745            8 :             if (promiseType) {
    3746            8 :                 for (const symbol of promiseType.getApparentProperties()) {
    3747            8 :                     if (typeChecker.isValidPropertyAccessForCompletions(propertyAccess, promiseType, symbol)) {
    3748            8 :                         addPropertySymbol(symbol, /*insertAwait*/ true, insertQuestionDot);
    3749            8 :                     }
    3750            8 :                 }
    3751            8 :             }
    3752            8 :         }
    3753            8 :     }
    3754            8 : 
    3755            8 :     function addPropertySymbol(symbol: Symbol, insertAwait: boolean, insertQuestionDot: boolean) {
    3756            8 :         // For a computed property with an accessible name like `Symbol.iterator`,
    3757            8 :         // we'll add a completion for the *name* `Symbol` instead of for the property.
    3758            8 :         // If this is e.g. [Symbol.iterator], add a completion for `Symbol`.
    3759            8 :         const computedPropertyName = firstDefined(symbol.declarations, decl => tryCast(getNameOfDeclaration(decl), isComputedPropertyName));
    3760            8 :         if (computedPropertyName) {
    3761            8 :             const leftMostName = getLeftMostName(computedPropertyName.expression); // The completion is for `Symbol`, not `iterator`.
    3762            8 :             const nameSymbol = leftMostName && typeChecker.getSymbolAtLocation(leftMostName);
    3763            8 :             // If this is nested like for `namespace N { export const sym = Symbol(); }`, we'll add the completion for `N`.
    3764            8 :             const firstAccessibleSymbol = nameSymbol && getFirstSymbolInChain(nameSymbol, contextToken, typeChecker);
    3765            8 :             const firstAccessibleSymbolId = firstAccessibleSymbol && getSymbolId(firstAccessibleSymbol);
    3766            8 :             if (firstAccessibleSymbolId && addToSeen(seenPropertySymbols, firstAccessibleSymbolId)) {
    3767            8 :                 const index = symbols.length;
    3768            8 :                 symbols.push(firstAccessibleSymbol);
    3769            8 :                 const moduleSymbol = firstAccessibleSymbol.parent;
    3770            8 :                 if (
    3771            8 :                     !moduleSymbol ||
    3772            8 :                     !isExternalModuleSymbol(moduleSymbol) ||
    3773            8 :                     typeChecker.tryGetMemberInModuleExportsAndProperties(firstAccessibleSymbol.name, moduleSymbol) !== firstAccessibleSymbol
    3774            8 :                 ) {
    3775            8 :                     symbolToOriginInfoMap[index] = { kind: getNullableSymbolOriginInfoKind(SymbolOriginInfoKind.SymbolMemberNoExport) };
    3776            8 :                 }
    3777            8 :                 else {
    3778            8 :                     const fileName = isExternalModuleNameRelative(stripQuotes(moduleSymbol.name)) ? getSourceFileOfModule(moduleSymbol)?.fileName : undefined;
    3779            8 :                     const { moduleSpecifier } = (importSpecifierResolver ||= codefix.createImportSpecifierResolver(sourceFile, program, host, preferences)).getModuleSpecifierForBestExportInfo(
    3780            8 :                         [{
    3781            8 :                             exportKind: ExportKind.Named,
    3782            8 :                             moduleFileName: fileName,
    3783            8 :                             isFromPackageJson: false,
    3784            8 :                             moduleSymbol,
    3785            8 :                             symbol: firstAccessibleSymbol,
    3786            8 :                             targetFlags: skipAlias(firstAccessibleSymbol, typeChecker).flags,
    3787            8 :                         }],
    3788            8 :                         position,
    3789            8 :                         isValidTypeOnlyAliasUseSite(location),
    3790            8 :                     ) || {};
    3791            8 : 
    3792            8 :                     if (moduleSpecifier) {
    3793            8 :                         const origin: SymbolOriginInfoResolvedExport = {
    3794            8 :                             kind: getNullableSymbolOriginInfoKind(SymbolOriginInfoKind.SymbolMemberExport),
    3795            8 :                             moduleSymbol,

    3797            8 :                             symbolName: firstAccessibleSymbol.name,
    3798            8 :                             exportName: firstAccessibleSymbol.name,
    3799            8 :                             fileName,
    3800            8 :                             moduleSpecifier,
    3801            8 :                         };
    3802            8 :                         symbolToOriginInfoMap[index] = origin;
    3803            8 :                     }
    3804            8 :                 }
    3805            8 :             }
    3806            8 :             else if (preferences.includeCompletionsWithInsertText) {
    3807            8 :                 if (firstAccessibleSymbolId && seenPropertySymbols.has(firstAccessibleSymbolId)) {
    3808            8 :                     return;

    3811            8 :                 addSymbolSortInfo(symbol);
    3812            8 :                 symbols.push(symbol);
    3813            8 :             }
    3814            8 :         }
    3815            8 :         else {
    3816            8 :             addSymbolOriginInfo(symbol);
    3817            8 :             addSymbolSortInfo(symbol);
    3818            8 :             symbols.push(symbol);
    3819            8 :         }

    3823            8 :                 symbolToSortTextMap[getSymbolId(symbol)] = SortText.LocalDeclarationPriority;
    3824            8 :             }

    3828            8 :             if (preferences.includeCompletionsWithInsertText) {

    3831            8 :                 }

    3834            8 :                 }

    3848            8 :     function tryGetGlobalSymbols(): boolean {

    3856            8 :             || tryGetClassLikeCompletionSymbols()
    3857            8 :             || tryGetJsxCompletionSymbols()
    3858            8 :             || (getGlobalCompletions(), GlobalsSearch.Success);
    3859            8 :         return result === GlobalsSearch.Success;
