    3862            8 :     function tryGetConstructorCompletion(): GlobalsSearch {
    3863            8 :         if (!tryGetConstructorLikeCompletionContainer(contextToken)) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    3864            8 :         // no members, only keywords
    3865            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.None;
    3866            8 :         // Declaring new property/method/accessor
    3867            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation = true;
    3868            8 :         // Has keywords for constructor parameter
    3869            8 :         keywordFilters = KeywordCompletionFilters.ConstructorParameterKeywords;
    3870            8 :         return GlobalsSearch.Success;
    3871            8 :     }

    3873            8 :     function tryGetJsxCompletionSymbols(): GlobalsSearch {
    3874            8 :         const jsxContainer = tryGetContainingJsxElement(contextToken);
    3875            8 :         // Cursor is inside a JSX self-closing element or opening element

    3879            8 :         symbols = concatenate(symbols, filterJsxAttributes(getPropertiesForObjectExpression(attrsType, completionsType, jsxContainer.attributes, typeChecker), jsxContainer.attributes.properties));
    3880            8 :         setSortTextToOptionalMember();

    3882            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation = false;

    3886            8 :     function tryGetImportCompletionSymbols(): GlobalsSearch {
    3887            8 :         if (!importStatementCompletion) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    3888            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation = true;
    3889            8 :         collectAutoImports();

    3893            8 :     function getGlobalCompletions(): void {
    3894            8 :         keywordFilters = tryGetFunctionLikeBodyCompletionContainer(contextToken) ? KeywordCompletionFilters.FunctionLikeBodyKeywords : KeywordCompletionFilters.All;
    3895            8 : 
    3896            8 :         // Get all entities in the current scope.
    3897            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.Global;
    3898            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation = isNewIdentifierDefinitionLocation();
    3899            8 : 
    3900            8 :         if (previousToken !== contextToken) {
    3901            8 :             Debug.assert(!!previousToken, "Expected 'contextToken' to be defined when different from 'previousToken'.");
    3902            8 :         }
    3903            8 :         // We need to find the node that will give us an appropriate scope to begin
    3904            8 :         // aggregating completion candidates. This is achieved in 'getScopeNode'
    3905            8 :         // by finding the first node that encompasses a position, accounting for whether a node
    3906            8 :         // is "complete" to decide whether a position belongs to the node.
    3907            8 :         //
    3908            8 :         // However, at the end of an identifier, we are interested in the scope of the identifier
    3909            8 :         // itself, but fall outside of the identifier. For instance:
    3910            8 :         //
    3911            8 :         //      xyz => x$
    3912            8 :         //
    3913            8 :         // the cursor is outside of both the 'x' and the arrow function 'xyz => x',
    3914            8 :         // so 'xyz' is not returned in our results.
    3915            8 :         //
    3916            8 :         // We define 'adjustedPosition' so that we may appropriately account for
    3917            8 :         // being at the end of an identifier. The intention is that if requesting completion
    3918            8 :         // at the end of an identifier, it should be effectively equivalent to requesting completion
    3919            8 :         // anywhere inside/at the beginning of the identifier. So in the previous case, the
    3920            8 :         // 'adjustedPosition' will work as if requesting completion in the following:
    3921            8 :         //
    3922            8 :         //      xyz => $x
    3923            8 :         //
    3924            8 :         // If previousToken !== contextToken, then
    3925            8 :         //   - 'contextToken' was adjusted to the token prior to 'previousToken'
    3926            8 :         //      because we were at the end of an identifier.
    3927            8 :         //   - 'previousToken' is defined.
    3928            8 :         const adjustedPosition = previousToken !== contextToken ?
    3929            8 :             previousToken.getStart() :
    3930            8 :             position;
    3931            8 : 
    3932            8 :         const scopeNode = getScopeNode(contextToken, adjustedPosition, sourceFile) || sourceFile;
    3933            8 :         isInSnippetScope = isSnippetScope(scopeNode);
    3934            8 : 
    3935            8 :         const symbolMeanings = (isTypeOnlyLocation ? SymbolFlags.None : SymbolFlags.Value) | SymbolFlags.Type | SymbolFlags.Namespace | SymbolFlags.Alias;
    3936            8 :         const typeOnlyAliasNeedsPromotion = previousToken && !isValidTypeOnlyAliasUseSite(previousToken);
    3937            8 : 
    3938            8 :         symbols = concatenate(symbols, typeChecker.getSymbolsInScope(scopeNode, symbolMeanings));
    3939            8 :         Debug.assertEachIsDefined(symbols, "getSymbolsInScope() should all be defined");
    3940            8 :         for (let i = 0; i < symbols.length; i++) {
    3941            8 :             const symbol = symbols[i];
    3942            8 :             if (
    3943            8 :                 !typeChecker.isArgumentsSymbol(symbol) &&
    3944            8 :                 !some(symbol.declarations, d => d.getSourceFile() === sourceFile)
    3945            8 :             ) {
    3946            8 :                 symbolToSortTextMap[getSymbolId(symbol)] = SortText.GlobalsOrKeywords;
    3947            8 :             }
    3948            8 :             if (typeOnlyAliasNeedsPromotion && !(symbol.flags & SymbolFlags.Value)) {
    3949            8 :                 const typeOnlyAliasDeclaration = symbol.declarations && find(symbol.declarations, isTypeOnlyImportDeclaration);
    3950            8 :                 if (typeOnlyAliasDeclaration) {
    3951            8 :                     const origin: SymbolOriginInfoTypeOnlyImport = { kind: SymbolOriginInfoKind.TypeOnlyAlias, declaration: typeOnlyAliasDeclaration };
    3952            8 :                     symbolToOriginInfoMap[i] = origin;
    3953            8 :                 }
    3954            8 :             }
    3955            8 :         }
    3956            8 : 
    3957            8 :         // Need to insert 'this.' before properties of `this` type, so only do that if `includeInsertTextCompletions`
    3958            8 :         if (preferences.includeCompletionsWithInsertText && scopeNode.kind !== SyntaxKind.SourceFile) {
    3959            8 :             const thisType = typeChecker.tryGetThisTypeAt(scopeNode, /*includeGlobalThis*/ false, isClassLike(scopeNode.parent) ? scopeNode as ThisContainer : undefined);
    3960            8 :             if (thisType && !isProbablyGlobalType(thisType, sourceFile, typeChecker)) {
    3961            8 :                 for (const symbol of getPropertiesForCompletion(thisType, typeChecker)) {
    3962            8 :                     symbolToOriginInfoMap[symbols.length] = { kind: SymbolOriginInfoKind.ThisType };
    3963            8 :                     symbols.push(symbol);
    3964            8 :                     symbolToSortTextMap[getSymbolId(symbol)] = SortText.SuggestedClassMembers;
    3965            8 :                 }
    3966            8 :             }
    3967            8 :         }
    3968            8 :         collectAutoImports();
    3969            8 :         if (isTypeOnlyLocation) {
    3970            8 :             keywordFilters = contextToken && isAssertionExpression(contextToken.parent)
    3971            8 :                 ? KeywordCompletionFilters.TypeAssertionKeywords
    3972            8 :                 : KeywordCompletionFilters.TypeKeywords;
    3973            8 :         }
    3974            8 :     }
    3975            8 : 
    3976            8 :     function shouldOfferImportCompletions(): boolean {
    3977            8 :         // If already typing an import statement, provide completions for it.
    3978            8 :         if (importStatementCompletion) return true;
    3979            8 :         // If not already a module, must have modules enabled.
    3980            8 :         if (!preferences.includeCompletionsForModuleExports) return false;
    3981            8 :         // If already using ES modules, OK to continue using them.
    3982            8 :         if (sourceFile.externalModuleIndicator || sourceFile.commonJsModuleIndicator) return true;
    3983            8 :         // If module transpilation is enabled or we're targeting es6 or above, or not emitting, OK.
    3984            8 :         if (compilerOptionsIndicateEsModules(program.getCompilerOptions())) return true;
    3985            8 :         // If some file is using ES6 modules, assume that it's OK to add more.
    3986            8 :         return program.getSymlinkCache?.().hasAnySymlinks() ||
    3987            8 :             !!program.getCompilerOptions().paths ||
    3988            8 :             programContainsModules(program);
    3989            8 :     }

    3991            8 :     function isSnippetScope(scopeNode: Node): boolean {

    3993            8 :             case SyntaxKind.SourceFile:
    3994            8 :             case SyntaxKind.TemplateExpression:
    3995            8 :             case SyntaxKind.JsxExpression:
    3996            8 :             case SyntaxKind.Block:
    3997            8 :                 return true;
    3998            8 :             default:
    3999            8 :                 return isStatement(scopeNode);
    4000            8 :         }
    4001            8 :     }

    4003            8 :     function isTypeOnlyCompletion(): boolean {
    4004            8 :         return insideJsDocTagTypeExpression
    4005            8 :             || insideJsDocImportTag
    4006            8 :             || !!importStatementCompletion && isTypeOnlyImportOrExportDeclaration(location.parent)
    4007            8 :             || !isContextTokenValueLocation(contextToken) &&
    4008            8 :                 (isPossiblyTypeArgumentPosition(contextToken, sourceFile, typeChecker)
    4009            8 :                     || isPartOfTypeNode(location)
    4010            8 :                     || isContextTokenTypeLocation(contextToken));
    4011            8 :     }

    4013            8 :     function isContextTokenValueLocation(contextToken: Node) {
    4014            8 :         return contextToken &&
    4015            8 :             ((contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.TypeOfKeyword &&
    4016            8 :                 (contextToken.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.TypeQuery || isTypeOfExpression(contextToken.parent))) ||
    4017            8 :                 (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.AssertsKeyword && contextToken.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.TypePredicate));
    4018            8 :     }

    4020            8 :     function isContextTokenTypeLocation(contextToken: Node): boolean {
    4021            8 :         if (contextToken) {
    4022            8 :             const parentKind = contextToken.parent.kind;
    4023            8 :             switch (contextToken.kind) {
    4024            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ColonToken:
    4025            8 :                     return parentKind === SyntaxKind.PropertyDeclaration ||
    4026            8 :                         parentKind === SyntaxKind.PropertySignature ||
    4027            8 :                         parentKind === SyntaxKind.Parameter ||
    4028            8 :                         parentKind === SyntaxKind.VariableDeclaration ||
    4029            8 :                         isFunctionLikeKind(parentKind);
    4030            8 : 
    4031            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.EqualsToken:
    4032            8 :                     return parentKind === SyntaxKind.TypeAliasDeclaration || parentKind === SyntaxKind.TypeParameter;
    4033            8 : 
    4034            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.AsKeyword:
    4035            8 :                     return parentKind === SyntaxKind.AsExpression;
    4036            8 : 
    4037            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.LessThanToken:
    4038            8 :                     return parentKind === SyntaxKind.TypeReference ||
    4039            8 :                         parentKind === SyntaxKind.TypeAssertionExpression;
    4040            8 : 
    4041            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ExtendsKeyword:
    4042            8 :                     return parentKind === SyntaxKind.TypeParameter;
    4043            8 : 
    4044            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.SatisfiesKeyword:
    4045            8 :                     return parentKind === SyntaxKind.SatisfiesExpression;
    4046            8 :             }
    4047            8 :         }
    4048            8 :         return false;
    4049            8 :     }

    4051            8 :     /** Mutates `symbols`, `symbolToOriginInfoMap`, and `symbolToSortTextMap` */
    4052            8 :     function collectAutoImports() {
    4053            8 :         if (!shouldOfferImportCompletions()) return;
    4054            8 :         Debug.assert(!detailsEntryId?.data, "Should not run 'collectAutoImports' when faster path is available via `data`");
    4055            8 :         if (detailsEntryId && !detailsEntryId.source) {
    4056            8 :             // Asking for completion details for an item that is not an auto-import
    4057            8 :             return;
    4058            8 :         }
    4059            8 : 
    4060            8 :         flags |= CompletionInfoFlags.MayIncludeAutoImports;
    4061            8 :         // import { type | -> token text should be blank
    4062            8 :         const isAfterTypeOnlyImportSpecifierModifier = previousToken === contextToken
    4063            8 :             && importStatementCompletion;
    4064            8 : 
    4065            8 :         const lowerCaseTokenText = isAfterTypeOnlyImportSpecifierModifier ? "" :
    4066            8 :             previousToken && isIdentifier(previousToken) ? previousToken.text.toLowerCase() :
    4067            8 :             "";

    4069            8 :         const moduleSpecifierCache = host.getModuleSpecifierCache?.();

    4072            8 :         const packageJsonFilter = detailsEntryId ? undefined : createPackageJsonImportFilter(sourceFile, preferences, host);
    4073            8 :         resolvingModuleSpecifiers(
    4074            8 :             "collectAutoImports",
    4075            8 :             host,
    4076            8 :             importSpecifierResolver ||= codefix.createImportSpecifierResolver(sourceFile, program, host, preferences),
    4077            8 :             program,
    4078            8 :             position,
    4079            8 :             preferences,
    4080            8 :             !!importStatementCompletion,
    4081            8 :             isValidTypeOnlyAliasUseSite(location),
    4082            8 :             context => {
    4083            8 :                 exportInfo.search(
    4084            8 :                     sourceFile.path,
    4085            8 :                     /*preferCapitalized*/ isRightOfOpenTag,
    4086            8 :                     (symbolName, targetFlags) => {
    4087            8 :                         if (!isIdentifierText(symbolName, getEmitScriptTarget(host.getCompilationSettings()))) return false;
    4088            8 :                         if (!detailsEntryId && isStringANonContextualKeyword(symbolName)) return false;
    4089            8 :                         if (!isTypeOnlyLocation && !importStatementCompletion && !(targetFlags & SymbolFlags.Value)) return false;
    4090            8 :                         if (isTypeOnlyLocation && !(targetFlags & (SymbolFlags.Module | SymbolFlags.Type))) return false;
    4091            8 :                         // Do not try to auto-import something with a lowercase first letter for a JSX tag
    4092            8 :                         const firstChar = symbolName.charCodeAt(0);
    4093            8 :                         if (isRightOfOpenTag && (firstChar < CharacterCodes.A || firstChar > CharacterCodes.Z)) return false;
    4094            8 : 
    4095            8 :                         if (detailsEntryId) return true;
    4096            8 :                         return charactersFuzzyMatchInString(symbolName, lowerCaseTokenText);
    4097            8 :                     },
    4098            8 :                     (info, symbolName, isFromAmbientModule, exportMapKey) => {
    4099            8 :                         if (detailsEntryId && !some(info, i => detailsEntryId.source === stripQuotes(i.moduleSymbol.name))) {
    4100            8 :                             return;
    4101            8 :                         }
    4102            8 : 
    4103            8 :                         // Do a relatively cheap check to bail early if all re-exports are non-importable
    4104            8 :                         // due to file location or package.json dependency filtering. For non-node16+
    4105            8 :                         // module resolution modes, getting past this point guarantees that we'll be
    4106            8 :                         // able to generate a suitable module specifier, so we can safely show a completion,
    4107            8 :                         // even if we defer computing the module specifier.
    4108            8 :                         info = filter(info, isImportableExportInfo);
    4109            8 :                         if (!info.length) {
    4110            8 :                             return;
    4111            8 :                         }
    4112            8 : 
    4113            8 :                         // In node16+, module specifier resolution can fail due to modules being blocked
    4114            8 :                         // by package.json `exports`. If that happens, don't show a completion item.
    4115            8 :                         // N.B. in this resolution mode we always try to resolve module specifiers here,
    4116            8 :                         // because we have to know now if it's going to fail so we can omit the completion
    4117            8 :                         // from the list.
    4118            8 :                         const result = context.tryResolve(info, isFromAmbientModule) || {};
    4119            8 :                         if (result === "failed") return;
    4120            8 :

    4133            8 : 
    4134            8 :                         pushAutoImportSymbol(symbol, {

    4177            8 :     function pushAutoImportSymbol(symbol: Symbol, origin: SymbolOriginInfoResolvedExport | SymbolOriginInfoExport) {
    4178            8 :         const symbolId = getSymbolId(symbol);
    4179            8 :         if (symbolToSortTextMap[symbolId] === SortText.GlobalsOrKeywords) {
    4180            8 :             // If an auto-importable symbol is available as a global, don't add the auto import
    4181            8 :             return;
    4182            8 :         }
    4183            8 :         symbolToOriginInfoMap[symbols.length] = origin;
    4184            8 :         symbolToSortTextMap[symbolId] = importStatementCompletion ? SortText.LocationPriority : SortText.AutoImportSuggestions;
    4185            8 :         symbols.push(symbol);
    4186            8 :     }

    4188            8 :     /* Mutates `symbols` and `symbolToOriginInfoMap`. */
    4189            8 :     function collectObjectLiteralMethodSymbols(members: Symbol[], enclosingDeclaration: ObjectLiteralExpression): void {
    4190            8 :         // TODO: support JS files.
    4191            8 :         if (isInJSFile(location)) {
    4192            8 :             return;
    4193            8 :         }
    4194            8 :         members.forEach(member => {
    4195            8 :             if (!isObjectLiteralMethodSymbol(member)) {
    4196            8 :                 return;
    4197            8 :             }
    4198            8 :             const displayName = getCompletionEntryDisplayNameForSymbol(
    4199            8 :                 member,
    4200            8 :                 getEmitScriptTarget(compilerOptions),
    4201            8 :                 /*origin*/ undefined,
    4202            8 :                 CompletionKind.ObjectPropertyDeclaration,
    4203            8 :                 /*jsxIdentifierExpected*/ false,
    4204            8 :             );
    4205            8 :             if (!displayName) {
    4206            8 :                 return;
    4207            8 :             }
    4208            8 :             const { name } = displayName;
    4209            8 :             const entryProps = getEntryForObjectLiteralMethodCompletion(
    4210            8 :                 member,
    4211            8 :                 name,
    4212            8 :                 enclosingDeclaration,
    4213            8 :                 program,
    4214            8 :                 host,
    4215            8 :                 compilerOptions,
    4216            8 :                 preferences,
    4217            8 :                 formatContext,
    4218            8 :             );
    4219            8 :             if (!entryProps) {
    4220            8 :                 return;
    4221            8 :             }
    4222            8 :             const origin: SymbolOriginInfoObjectLiteralMethod = { kind: SymbolOriginInfoKind.ObjectLiteralMethod, ...entryProps };
    4223            8 :             flags |= CompletionInfoFlags.MayIncludeMethodSnippets;
    4224            8 :             symbolToOriginInfoMap[symbols.length] = origin;
    4225            8 :             symbols.push(member);
    4226            8 :         });
    4227            8 :     }
    4228            8 : 
    4229            8 :     function isObjectLiteralMethodSymbol(symbol: Symbol): boolean {
    4230            8 :         /*
    4231            8 :             For an object type
    4232            8 :             `type Foo = {
    4233            8 :                 bar(x: number): void;
    4234            8 :                 foo: (x: string) => string;
    4235            8 :             }`,
    4236            8 :             `bar` will have symbol flag `Method`,
    4237            8 :             `foo` will have symbol flag `Property`.
    4238            8 :         */
    4239            8 :         if (!(symbol.flags & (SymbolFlags.Property | SymbolFlags.Method))) {
    4240            8 :             return false;
    4241            8 :         }
    4242            8 :         return true;
    4243            8 :     }
    4244            8 : 
    4245            8 :     /**
    4246            8 :      * Finds the first node that "embraces" the position, so that one may
    4247            8 :      * accurately aggregate locals from the closest containing scope.
    4248            8 :      */
    4249            8 :     function getScopeNode(initialToken: Node | undefined, position: number, sourceFile: SourceFile) {
    4250            8 :         let scope: Node | undefined = initialToken;
    4251            8 :         while (scope && !positionBelongsToNode(scope, position, sourceFile)) {
    4252            8 :             scope = scope.parent;
    4253            8 :         }
    4254            8 :         return scope;
    4255            8 :     }
    4256            8 : 
    4257            8 :     function isCompletionListBlocker(contextToken: Node): boolean {
    4258            8 :         const start = timestamp();
    4259            8 :         const result = isInStringOrRegularExpressionOrTemplateLiteral(contextToken) ||
    4260            8 :             isSolelyIdentifierDefinitionLocation(contextToken) ||
    4261            8 :             isDotOfNumericLiteral(contextToken) ||
    4262            8 :             isInJsxText(contextToken) ||
    4263            8 :             isBigIntLiteral(contextToken);
    4264            8 :         log("getCompletionsAtPosition: isCompletionListBlocker: " + (timestamp() - start));
    4265            8 :         return result;
    4266            8 :     }
    4267            8 : 
    4268            8 :     function isInJsxText(contextToken: Node): boolean {
    4269            8 :         if (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxText) {
    4270            8 :             return true;
    4271            8 :         }
    4272            8 : 
    4273            8 :         if (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.GreaterThanToken && contextToken.parent) {
    4274            8 :             // <Component<string> /**/ />
    4275            8 :             // <Component<string> /**/ ><Component>
    4276            8 :             // - contextToken: GreaterThanToken (before cursor)
    4277            8 :             // - location: JsxSelfClosingElement or JsxOpeningElement
    4278            8 :             // - contextToken.parent === location
    4279            8 :             if (location === contextToken.parent && (location.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxOpeningElement || location.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxSelfClosingElement)) {
    4280            8 :                 return false;
    4281            8 :             }
    4282            8 : 
    4283            8 :             if (contextToken.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxOpeningElement) {
    4284            8 :                 // <div>/**/
    4285            8 :                 // - contextToken: GreaterThanToken (before cursor)
    4286            8 :                 // - location: JSXElement
    4287            8 :                 // - different parents (JSXOpeningElement, JSXElement)
    4288            8 :                 return location.parent.kind !== SyntaxKind.JsxOpeningElement;
    4289            8 :             }
    4290            8 : 
    4291            8 :             if (contextToken.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxClosingElement || contextToken.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxSelfClosingElement) {
    4292            8 :                 return !!contextToken.parent.parent && contextToken.parent.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxElement;
    4293            8 :             }
    4294            8 :         }
    4295            8 :         return false;
    4296            8 :     }
    4297            8 : 
    4298            8 :     function isNewIdentifierDefinitionLocation(): boolean {
    4299            8 :         if (contextToken) {
    4300            8 :             const containingNodeKind = contextToken.parent.kind;
    4301            8 :             const tokenKind = keywordForNode(contextToken);
    4302            8 :             // Previous token may have been a keyword that was converted to an identifier.
    4303            8 :             // dprint-ignore
    4304            8 :             switch (tokenKind) {
    4305            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.CommaToken:
    4306            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.CallExpression               // func( a, |
    4307            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.Constructor                  // constructor( a, |   /* public, protected, private keywords are allowed here, so show completion */
    4308            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.NewExpression                // new C(a, |
    4309            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ArrayLiteralExpression       // [a, |
    4310            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.BinaryExpression             // const x = (a, |
    4311            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.FunctionType                 // var x: (s: string, list|
    4312            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ObjectLiteralExpression;     // const obj = { x, |
    4313            8 : 
    4314            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.OpenParenToken:
    4315            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.CallExpression               // func( |
    4316            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.Constructor                  // constructor( |
    4317            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.NewExpression                // new C(a|
    4318            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ParenthesizedExpression      // const x = (a|
    4319            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ParenthesizedType;           // function F(pred: (a| /* this can become an arrow function, where 'a' is the argument */
    4320            8 : 
    4321            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.OpenBracketToken:
    4322            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ArrayLiteralExpression       // [ |
    4323            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.IndexSignature               // [ | : string ]
    4324            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ComputedPropertyName;         // [ |    /* this can become an index signature */
    4325            8 : 
    4326            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ModuleKeyword:                                            // module |
    4327            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.NamespaceKeyword:                                         // namespace |
    4328            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.ImportKeyword:                                            // import |
    4329            8 :                     return true;
    4330            8 : 
    4331            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.DotToken:
    4332            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ModuleDeclaration;           // module A.|
    4333            8 : 
    4334            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.OpenBraceToken:
    4335            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ClassDeclaration             // class A { |
    4336            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ObjectLiteralExpression;     // const obj = { |
    4337            8 : 
    4338            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.EqualsToken:
    4339            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.VariableDeclaration          // const x = a|
    4340            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.BinaryExpression;            // x = a|
    4341            8 : 
    4342            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TemplateHead:
    4343            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.TemplateExpression;          // `aa ${|
    4344            8 : 
    4345            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.TemplateMiddle:
    4346            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.TemplateSpan;                // `aa ${10} dd ${|
    4347            8 : 
    4348            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.AsyncKeyword:
    4349            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.MethodDeclaration            // const obj = { async c|()
    4350            8 :                         || containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ShorthandPropertyAssignment; // const obj = { async c|
    4351            8 : 
    4352            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.AsteriskToken:
    4353            8 :                     return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.MethodDeclaration;           // const obj = { * c|
    4354            8 :             }
    4355            8 : 
    4356            8 :             if (isClassMemberCompletionKeyword(tokenKind)) {
    4357            8 :                 return true;
    4358            8 :             }
    4359            8 :         }
    4360            8 : 
    4361            8 :         return false;
    4362            8 :     }
    4363            8 : 
    4364            8 :     function isInStringOrRegularExpressionOrTemplateLiteral(contextToken: Node): boolean {
    4365            8 :         // To be "in" one of these literals, the position has to be:
    4366            8 :         //   1. entirely within the token text.
    4367            8 :         //   2. at the end position of an unterminated token.
    4368            8 :         //   3. at the end of a regular expression (due to trailing flags like '/foo/g').
    4369            8 :         return (isRegularExpressionLiteral(contextToken) || isStringTextContainingNode(contextToken)) && (
    4370            8 :             rangeContainsPositionExclusive(contextToken, position) ||
    4371            8 :             position === contextToken.end && (!!contextToken.isUnterminated || isRegularExpressionLiteral(contextToken))
    4372            8 :         );
    4373            8 :     }
    4374            8 : 
    4375            8 :     function tryGetObjectTypeLiteralInTypeArgumentCompletionSymbols(): GlobalsSearch | undefined {
    4376            8 :         const typeLiteralNode = tryGetTypeLiteralNode(contextToken);
    4377            8 :         if (!typeLiteralNode) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4378            8 : 
    4379            8 :         const intersectionTypeNode = isIntersectionTypeNode(typeLiteralNode.parent) ? typeLiteralNode.parent : undefined;
    4380            8 :         const containerTypeNode = intersectionTypeNode || typeLiteralNode;
    4381            8 : 
    4382            8 :         const containerExpectedType = getConstraintOfTypeArgumentProperty(containerTypeNode, typeChecker);
    4383            8 :         if (!containerExpectedType) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4384            8 : 
    4385            8 :         const containerActualType = typeChecker.getTypeFromTypeNode(containerTypeNode);
    4386            8 : 
    4387            8 :         const members = getPropertiesForCompletion(containerExpectedType, typeChecker);
    4388            8 :         const existingMembers = getPropertiesForCompletion(containerActualType, typeChecker);
    4389            8 : 
    4390            8 :         const existingMemberEscapedNames = new Set<__String>();
    4391            8 :         existingMembers.forEach(s => existingMemberEscapedNames.add(s.escapedName));
    4392            8 : 
    4393            8 :         symbols = concatenate(symbols, filter(members, s => !existingMemberEscapedNames.has(s.escapedName)));
    4394            8 : 
    4395            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.ObjectPropertyDeclaration;
    4396            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation = true;
    4397            8 : 
    4398            8 :         return GlobalsSearch.Success;
    4399            8 :     }
    4400            8 : 
    4401            8 :     /**
    4402            8 :      * Aggregates relevant symbols for completion in object literals and object binding patterns.
    4403            8 :      * Relevant symbols are stored in the captured 'symbols' variable.
    4404            8 :      *
    4405            8 :      * @returns true if 'symbols' was successfully populated; false otherwise.
    4406            8 :      */
    4407            8 :     function tryGetObjectLikeCompletionSymbols(): GlobalsSearch | undefined {
    4408            8 :         if (contextToken?.kind === SyntaxKind.DotDotDotToken) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4409            8 :         const symbolsStartIndex = symbols.length;
    4410            8 :         const objectLikeContainer = tryGetObjectLikeCompletionContainer(contextToken, position, sourceFile);
    4411            8 :         if (!objectLikeContainer) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4412            8 : 
    4413            8 :         // We're looking up possible property names from contextual/inferred/declared type.
    4414            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.ObjectPropertyDeclaration;
    4415            8 : 
    4416            8 :         let typeMembers: Symbol[] | undefined;
    4417            8 :         let existingMembers: readonly Declaration[] | undefined;
    4418            8 : 
    4419            8 :         if (objectLikeContainer.kind === SyntaxKind.ObjectLiteralExpression) {
    4420            8 :             const instantiatedType = tryGetObjectLiteralContextualType(objectLikeContainer, typeChecker);
    4421            8 : 
    4422            8 :             // Check completions for Object property value shorthand
    4423            8 :             if (instantiatedType === undefined) {
    4424            8 :                 if (objectLikeContainer.flags & NodeFlags.InWithStatement) {
    4425            8 :                     return GlobalsSearch.Fail;
    4426            8 :                 }
    4427            8 :                 return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4428            8 :             }
    4429            8 :             const completionsType = typeChecker.getContextualType(objectLikeContainer, ContextFlags.Completions);
    4430            8 :             const hasStringIndexType = (completionsType || instantiatedType).getStringIndexType();
    4431            8 :             const hasNumberIndextype = (completionsType || instantiatedType).getNumberIndexType();
    4432            8 :             isNewIdentifierLocation = !!hasStringIndexType || !!hasNumberIndextype;
    4433            8 :             typeMembers = getPropertiesForObjectExpression(instantiatedType, completionsType, objectLikeContainer, typeChecker);
    4434            8 :             existingMembers = objectLikeContainer.properties;
    4435            8 : 
    4436            8 :             if (typeMembers.length === 0) {
    4437            8 :                 // Edge case: If NumberIndexType exists
    4438            8 :                 if (!hasNumberIndextype) {
    4439            8 :                     return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4440            8 :                 }
    4441            8 :             }
    4442            8 :         }
    4443            8 :         else {
    4444            8 :             Debug.assert(objectLikeContainer.kind === SyntaxKind.ObjectBindingPattern);
    4445            8 :             // We are *only* completing on properties from the type being destructured.
    4446            8 :             isNewIdentifierLocation = false;
    4447            8 : 
    4448            8 :             const rootDeclaration = getRootDeclaration(objectLikeContainer.parent);
    4449            8 :             if (!isVariableLike(rootDeclaration)) return Debug.fail("Root declaration is not variable-like.");
    4450            8 : 
    4451            8 :             // We don't want to complete using the type acquired by the shape
    4452            8 :             // of the binding pattern; we are only interested in types acquired
    4453            8 :             // through type declaration or inference.
    4454            8 :             // Also proceed if rootDeclaration is a parameter and if its containing function expression/arrow function is contextually typed -
    4455            8 :             // type of parameter will flow in from the contextual type of the function
    4456            8 :             let canGetType = hasInitializer(rootDeclaration) || !!getEffectiveTypeAnnotationNode(rootDeclaration) || rootDeclaration.parent.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.ForOfStatement;
    4457            8 :             if (!canGetType && rootDeclaration.kind === SyntaxKind.Parameter) {
    4458            8 :                 if (isExpression(rootDeclaration.parent)) {
    4459            8 :                     canGetType = !!typeChecker.getContextualType(rootDeclaration.parent as Expression);
    4460            8 :                 }
    4461            8 :                 else if (rootDeclaration.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.MethodDeclaration || rootDeclaration.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.SetAccessor) {
    4462            8 :                     canGetType = isExpression(rootDeclaration.parent.parent) && !!typeChecker.getContextualType(rootDeclaration.parent.parent as Expression);
    4463            8 :                 }
    4464            8 :             }
    4465            8 :             if (canGetType) {
    4466            8 :                 const typeForObject = typeChecker.getTypeAtLocation(objectLikeContainer);
    4467            8 :                 if (!typeForObject) return GlobalsSearch.Fail;
    4468            8 :                 typeMembers = typeChecker.getPropertiesOfType(typeForObject).filter(propertySymbol => {
    4469            8 :                     return typeChecker.isPropertyAccessible(objectLikeContainer, /*isSuper*/ false, /*isWrite*/ false, typeForObject, propertySymbol);
    4470            8 :                 });
    4471            8 :                 existingMembers = objectLikeContainer.elements;
    4472            8 :             }
    4473            8 :         }
    4474            8 : 
    4475            8 :         if (typeMembers && typeMembers.length > 0) {
    4476            8 :             // Add filtered items to the completion list
    4477            8 :             const filteredMembers = filterObjectMembersList(typeMembers, Debug.checkDefined(existingMembers));
    4478            8 :             symbols = concatenate(symbols, filteredMembers);
    4479            8 :             setSortTextToOptionalMember();
    4480            8 :             if (
    4481            8 :                 objectLikeContainer.kind === SyntaxKind.ObjectLiteralExpression
    4482            8 :                 && preferences.includeCompletionsWithObjectLiteralMethodSnippets
    4483            8 :                 && preferences.includeCompletionsWithInsertText
    4484            8 :             ) {
    4485            8 :                 transformObjectLiteralMembersSortText(symbolsStartIndex);
    4486            8 :                 collectObjectLiteralMethodSymbols(filteredMembers, objectLikeContainer);
    4487            8 :             }
    4488            8 :         }
    4489            8 : 
    4490            8 :         return GlobalsSearch.Success;
    4491            8 :     }
    4492            8 : 
    4493            8 :     /**
    4494            8 :      * Aggregates relevant symbols for completion in import clauses and export clauses
    4495            8 :      * whose declarations have a module specifier; for instance, symbols will be aggregated for
    4496            8 :      *
    4497            8 :      *      import { | } from "moduleName";
    4498            8 :      *      export { a as foo, | } from "moduleName";
    4499            8 :      *
    4500            8 :      * but not for
    4501            8 :      *
    4502            8 :      *      export { | };
    4503            8 :      *
    4504            8 :      * Relevant symbols are stored in the captured 'symbols' variable.
    4505            8 :      */
    4506            8 :     function tryGetImportOrExportClauseCompletionSymbols(): GlobalsSearch {
    4507            8 :         if (!contextToken) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4508            8 : 
    4509            8 :         // `import { |` or `import { a as 0, | }` or `import { type | }`
    4510            8 :         const namedImportsOrExports = contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.OpenBraceToken || contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.CommaToken ? tryCast(contextToken.parent, isNamedImportsOrExports) :
    4511            8 :             isTypeKeywordTokenOrIdentifier(contextToken) ? tryCast(contextToken.parent.parent, isNamedImportsOrExports) : undefined;
    4512            8 : 
    4513            8 :         if (!namedImportsOrExports) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4514            8 : 
    4515            8 :         // We can at least offer `type` at `import { |`
    4516            8 :         if (!isTypeKeywordTokenOrIdentifier(contextToken)) {
    4517            8 :             keywordFilters = KeywordCompletionFilters.TypeKeyword;
    4518            8 :         }
    4519            8 : 
    4520            8 :         // try to show exported member for imported/re-exported module
    4521            8 :         const { moduleSpecifier } = namedImportsOrExports.kind === SyntaxKind.NamedImports ? namedImportsOrExports.parent.parent : namedImportsOrExports.parent;
    4522            8 :         if (!moduleSpecifier) {
    4523            8 :             isNewIdentifierLocation = true;
    4524            8 :             return namedImportsOrExports.kind === SyntaxKind.NamedImports ? GlobalsSearch.Fail : GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4525            8 :         }
    4526            8 :         const moduleSpecifierSymbol = typeChecker.getSymbolAtLocation(moduleSpecifier); // TODO: GH#18217
    4527            8 :         if (!moduleSpecifierSymbol) {
    4528            8 :             isNewIdentifierLocation = true;
    4529            8 :             return GlobalsSearch.Fail;
    4530            8 :         }
    4531            8 : 
    4532            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.MemberLike;
    4533            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation = false;
    4534            8 :         const exports = typeChecker.getExportsAndPropertiesOfModule(moduleSpecifierSymbol);
    4535            8 :         const existing = new Set((namedImportsOrExports.elements as NodeArray<ImportOrExportSpecifier>).filter(n => !isCurrentlyEditingNode(n)).map(n => moduleExportNameTextEscaped(n.propertyName || n.name)));
    4536            8 :         const uniques = exports.filter(e => e.escapedName !== InternalSymbolName.Default && !existing.has(e.escapedName));
    4537            8 :         symbols = concatenate(symbols, uniques);
    4538            8 :         if (!uniques.length) {
    4539            8 :             // If there's nothing else to import, don't offer `type` either
    4540            8 :             keywordFilters = KeywordCompletionFilters.None;
    4541            8 :         }
    4542            8 :         return GlobalsSearch.Success;
    4543            8 :     }
    4544            8 : 
    4545            8 :     /**
    4546            8 :      * import { x } from "foo" with { | }
    4547            8 :      */
    4548            8 :     function tryGetImportAttributesCompletionSymbols(): GlobalsSearch {
    4549            8 :         if (contextToken === undefined) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4550            8 : 
    4551            8 :         const importAttributes = contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.OpenBraceToken || contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.CommaToken ? tryCast(contextToken.parent, isImportAttributes) :
    4552            8 :             contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.ColonToken ? tryCast(contextToken.parent.parent, isImportAttributes) : undefined;
    4553            8 :         if (importAttributes === undefined) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4554            8 : 
    4555            8 :         const existing = new Set(importAttributes.elements.map(getNameFromImportAttribute));
    4556            8 :         symbols = filter(typeChecker.getTypeAtLocation(importAttributes).getApparentProperties(), attr => !existing.has(attr.escapedName));
    4557            8 :         return GlobalsSearch.Success;
    4558            8 :     }
    4559            8 : 
    4560            8 :     /**
    4561            8 :      * Adds local declarations for completions in named exports:
    4562            8 :      *
    4563            8 :      *   export { | };
    4564            8 :      *
    4565            8 :      * Does not check for the absence of a module specifier (`export {} from "./other"`)
    4566            8 :      * because `tryGetImportOrExportClauseCompletionSymbols` runs first and handles that,
    4567            8 :      * preventing this function from running.
    4568            8 :      */
    4569            8 :     function tryGetLocalNamedExportCompletionSymbols(): GlobalsSearch {
    4570            8 :         const namedExports = contextToken && (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.OpenBraceToken || contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.CommaToken)
    4571            8 :             ? tryCast(contextToken.parent, isNamedExports)
    4572            8 :             : undefined;
    4573            8 : 
    4574            8 :         if (!namedExports) {
    4575            8 :             return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4576            8 :         }
    4577            8 : 
    4578            8 :         const localsContainer = findAncestor(namedExports, or(isSourceFile, isModuleDeclaration))!;
    4579            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.None;
    4580            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation = false;
    4581            8 :         localsContainer.locals?.forEach((symbol, name) => {
    4582            8 :             symbols.push(symbol);
    4583            8 :             if (localsContainer.symbol?.exports?.has(name)) {
    4584            8 :                 symbolToSortTextMap[getSymbolId(symbol)] = SortText.OptionalMember;
    4585            8 :             }
    4586            8 :         });
    4587            8 :         return GlobalsSearch.Success;
    4588            8 :     }
    4589            8 : 
    4590            8 :     /**
    4591            8 :      * Aggregates relevant symbols for completion in class declaration
    4592            8 :      * Relevant symbols are stored in the captured 'symbols' variable.
    4593            8 :      */
    4594            8 :     function tryGetClassLikeCompletionSymbols(): GlobalsSearch {
    4595            8 :         const decl = tryGetObjectTypeDeclarationCompletionContainer(sourceFile, contextToken, location, position);
    4596            8 :         if (!decl) return GlobalsSearch.Continue;
    4597            8 : 
    4598            8 :         // We're looking up possible property names from parent type.
    4599            8 :         completionKind = CompletionKind.MemberLike;
    4600            8 :         // Declaring new property/method/accessor
    4601            8 :         isNewIdentifierLocation = true;
    4602            8 :         keywordFilters = contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.AsteriskToken ? KeywordCompletionFilters.None :
    4603            8 :             isClassLike(decl) ? KeywordCompletionFilters.ClassElementKeywords : KeywordCompletionFilters.InterfaceElementKeywords;
    4604            8 : 
    4605            8 :         // If you're in an interface you don't want to repeat things from super-interface. So just stop here.
    4606            8 :         if (!isClassLike(decl)) return GlobalsSearch.Success;
    4607            8 : 
    4608            8 :         const classElement = contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.SemicolonToken ? contextToken.parent.parent : contextToken.parent;
    4609            8 :         let classElementModifierFlags = isClassElement(classElement) ? getEffectiveModifierFlags(classElement) : ModifierFlags.None;
    4610            8 :         // If this is context token is not something we are editing now, consider if this would lead to be modifier
    4611            8 :         if (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.Identifier && !isCurrentlyEditingNode(contextToken)) {
    4612            8 :             switch (contextToken.getText()) {
    4613            8 :                 case "private":
    4614            8 :                     classElementModifierFlags = classElementModifierFlags | ModifierFlags.Private;
    4615            8 :                     break;
    4616            8 :                 case "static":
    4617            8 :                     classElementModifierFlags = classElementModifierFlags | ModifierFlags.Static;
    4618            8 :                     break;
    4619            8 :                 case "override":
    4620            8 :                     classElementModifierFlags = classElementModifierFlags | ModifierFlags.Override;
    4621            8 :                     break;
    4622            8 :             }
    4623            8 :         }
    4624            8 :         if (isClassStaticBlockDeclaration(classElement)) {
    4625            8 :             classElementModifierFlags |= ModifierFlags.Static;
    4626            8 :         }
    4627            8 : 
    4628            8 :         // No member list for private methods
    4629            8 :         if (!(classElementModifierFlags & ModifierFlags.Private)) {
    4630            8 :             // List of property symbols of base type that are not private and already implemented
    4631            8 :             const baseTypeNodes = isClassLike(decl) && classElementModifierFlags & ModifierFlags.Override ? singleElementArray(getEffectiveBaseTypeNode(decl)) : getAllSuperTypeNodes(decl);
    4632            8 :             const baseSymbols = flatMap(baseTypeNodes, baseTypeNode => {
    4633            8 :                 const type = typeChecker.getTypeAtLocation(baseTypeNode);
    4634            8 :                 return classElementModifierFlags & ModifierFlags.Static ?
    4635            8 :                     type?.symbol && typeChecker.getPropertiesOfType(typeChecker.getTypeOfSymbolAtLocation(type.symbol, decl)) :
    4636            8 :                     type && typeChecker.getPropertiesOfType(type);
    4637            8 :             });
    4638            8 :             symbols = concatenate(symbols, filterClassMembersList(baseSymbols, decl.members, classElementModifierFlags));
    4639            8 :             forEach(symbols, (symbol, index) => {
    4640            8 :                 const declaration = symbol?.valueDeclaration;
    4641            8 :                 if (declaration && isClassElement(declaration) && declaration.name && isComputedPropertyName(declaration.name)) {
    4642            8 :                     const origin: SymbolOriginInfoComputedPropertyName = {
    4643            8 :                         kind: SymbolOriginInfoKind.ComputedPropertyName,
    4644            8 :                         symbolName: typeChecker.symbolToString(symbol),
    4645            8 :                     };
    4646            8 :                     symbolToOriginInfoMap[index] = origin;
    4647            8 :                 }
    4648            8 :             });
    4649            8 :         }
    4650            8 :         return GlobalsSearch.Success;
    4651            8 :     }
    4652            8 : 
    4653            8 :     function isConstructorParameterCompletion(node: Node): boolean {
    4654            8 :         return !!node.parent && isParameter(node.parent) && isConstructorDeclaration(node.parent.parent)
    4655            8 :             && (isParameterPropertyModifier(node.kind) || isDeclarationName(node));
    4656            8 :     }

    4658            8 :     /**
    4659            8 :      * Returns the immediate owning class declaration of a context token,
    4660            8 :      * on the condition that one exists and that the context implies completion should be given.
    4661            8 :      */
    4662            8 :     function tryGetConstructorLikeCompletionContainer(contextToken: Node): ConstructorDeclaration | undefined {
    4663            8 :         if (contextToken) {
    4664            8 :             const parent = contextToken.parent;
    4665            8 :             switch (contextToken.kind) {
    4666            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.OpenParenToken:
    4667            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.CommaToken:
    4668            8 :                     return isConstructorDeclaration(contextToken.parent) ? contextToken.parent : undefined;
    4669            8 : 
    4670            8 :                 default:
    4671            8 :                     if (isConstructorParameterCompletion(contextToken)) {
    4672            8 :                         return parent.parent as ConstructorDeclaration;
    4673            8 :                     }
    4674            8 :             }
    4675            8 :         }
    4676            8 :         return undefined;
    4677            8 :     }

    4679            8 :     function tryGetFunctionLikeBodyCompletionContainer(contextToken: Node): FunctionLikeDeclaration | undefined {
    4680            8 :         if (contextToken) {
    4681            8 :             let prev: Node;
    4682            8 :             const container = findAncestor(contextToken.parent, (node: Node) => {
    4683            8 :                 if (isClassLike(node)) {
    4684            8 :                     return "quit";
    4685            8 :                 }
    4686            8 :                 if (isFunctionLikeDeclaration(node) && prev === node.body) {
    4687            8 :                     return true;
    4688            8 :                 }
    4689            8 :                 prev = node;
    4690            8 :                 return false;
    4691            8 :             });
    4692            8 :             return container && container as FunctionLikeDeclaration;
    4693            8 :         }
    4694            8 :     }

    4696            8 :     function tryGetContainingJsxElement(contextToken: Node): JsxOpeningLikeElement | undefined {
    4697            8 :         if (contextToken) {
    4698            8 :             const parent = contextToken.parent;
    4699            8 :             switch (contextToken.kind) {
    4700            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.GreaterThanToken: // End of a type argument list
    4701            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.LessThanSlashToken:
    4702            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.SlashToken:
    4703            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.Identifier:
    4704            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.PropertyAccessExpression:
    4705            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxAttributes:
    4706            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxAttribute:
    4707            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.JsxSpreadAttribute:
    4708            8 :                     if (parent && (parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxSelfClosingElement || parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxOpeningElement)) {
    4709            8 :                         if (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.GreaterThanToken) {
    4710            8 :                             const precedingToken = findPrecedingToken(contextToken.pos, sourceFile, /*startNode*/ undefined);
    4711            8 :                             if (!(parent as JsxOpeningLikeElement).typeArguments || (precedingToken && precedingToken.kind === SyntaxKind.SlashToken)) break;
    4712            8 :                         }
    4713            8 :                         return parent as JsxOpeningLikeElement;
    4714            8 :                     }
    4715            8 :                     else if (parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxAttribute) {
    4716            8 :                         // Currently we parse JsxOpeningLikeElement as:
    4717            8 :                         //      JsxOpeningLikeElement
    4718            8 :                         //          attributes: JsxAttributes
    4719            8 :                         //             properties: NodeArray<JsxAttributeLike>
    4720            8 :                         return parent.parent.parent as JsxOpeningLikeElement;
    4721            8 :                     }
    4722            8 :                     break;
    4723            8 : 
    4724            8 :                 // The context token is the closing } or " of an attribute, which means
    4725            8 :                 // its parent is a JsxExpression, whose parent is a JsxAttribute,
    4726            8 :                 // whose parent is a JsxOpeningLikeElement
    4727            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.StringLiteral:
    4728            8 :                     if (parent && ((parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxAttribute) || (parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxSpreadAttribute))) {
    4729            8 :                         // Currently we parse JsxOpeningLikeElement as:
    4730            8 :                         //      JsxOpeningLikeElement
    4731            8 :                         //          attributes: JsxAttributes
    4732            8 :                         //             properties: NodeArray<JsxAttributeLike>
    4733            8 :                         return parent.parent.parent as JsxOpeningLikeElement;
    4734            8 :                     }
    4735            8 : 
    4736            8 :                     break;
    4737            8 : 
    4738            8 :                 case SyntaxKind.CloseBraceToken:
    4739            8 :                     if (
    4740            8 :                         parent &&
    4741            8 :                         parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxExpression &&
    4742            8 :                         parent.parent && parent.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxAttribute
    4743            8 :                     ) {
    4744            8 :                         // Currently we parse JsxOpeningLikeElement as:
    4745            8 :                         //      JsxOpeningLikeElement
    4746            8 :                         //          attributes: JsxAttributes
    4747            8 :                         //             properties: NodeArray<JsxAttributeLike>
    4748            8 :                         //                  each JsxAttribute can have initializer as JsxExpression
    4749            8 :                         return parent.parent.parent.parent as JsxOpeningLikeElement;
    4750            8 :                     }
    4751            8 : 
    4752            8 :                     if (parent && parent.kind === SyntaxKind.JsxSpreadAttribute) {
    4753            8 :                         // Currently we parse JsxOpeningLikeElement as:
    4754            8 :                         //      JsxOpeningLikeElement
    4755            8 :                         //          attributes: JsxAttributes
    4756            8 :                         //             properties: NodeArray<JsxAttributeLike>
    4757            8 :                         return parent.parent.parent as JsxOpeningLikeElement;
    4758            8 :                     }
    4759            8 : 
    4760            8 :                     break;
    4761            8 :             }
    4762            8 :         }
    4763            8 :         return undefined;
    4764            8 :     }
    4765            8 : 
    4766            8 :     function isInDifferentLineThanContextToken(contextToken: Node, position: number): boolean {
    4767            8 :         return sourceFile.getLineEndOfPosition(contextToken.getEnd()) < position;
    4768            8 :     }

    4770            8 :     /**
    4771            8 :      * @returns true if we are certain that the currently edited location must define a new location; false otherwise.
    4772            8 :      */
    4773            8 :     function isSolelyIdentifierDefinitionLocation(contextToken: Node): boolean {
    4774            8 :         const parent = contextToken.parent;
    4775            8 :         const containingNodeKind = parent.kind;
    4776            8 :         // dprint-ignore
    4777            8 :         switch (contextToken.kind) {
    4778            8 :             case SyntaxKind.CommaToken:
    4779            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.VariableDeclaration ||
    4780            8 :                     isVariableDeclarationListButNotTypeArgument(contextToken) ||
    4781            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.VariableStatement ||
    4782            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.EnumDeclaration ||                        // enum a { foo, |
    4783            8 :                     isFunctionLikeButNotConstructor(containingNodeKind) ||
    4784            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.InterfaceDeclaration ||                   // interface A<T, |
    4785            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ArrayBindingPattern ||                    // var [x, y|
    4786            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.TypeAliasDeclaration ||                   // type Map, K, |
    4787            8 :                     // class A<T, |
    4788            8 :                     // var C = class D<T, |
    4789            8 :                     (isClassLike(parent) &&
    4790            8 :                         !!parent.typeParameters &&
    4791            8 :                         parent.typeParameters.end >= contextToken.pos);
    4792            8 : 
    4793            8 :             case SyntaxKind.DotToken:
    4794            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ArrayBindingPattern;                   // var [.|
    4795            8 : 
    4796            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ColonToken:
    4797            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.BindingElement;                        // var {x :html|
    4798            8 : 
    4799            8 :             case SyntaxKind.OpenBracketToken:
    4800            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ArrayBindingPattern;                   // var [x|
    4801            8 : 
    4802            8 :             case SyntaxKind.OpenParenToken:
    4803            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.CatchClause ||
    4804            8 :                     isFunctionLikeButNotConstructor(containingNodeKind);
    4805            8 : 
    4806            8 :             case SyntaxKind.OpenBraceToken:
    4807            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.EnumDeclaration;                       // enum a { |
    4808            8 : 
    4809            8 :             case SyntaxKind.LessThanToken:
    4810            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ClassDeclaration ||                    // class A< |
    4811            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ClassExpression ||                        // var C = class D< |
    4812            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.InterfaceDeclaration ||                   // interface A< |
    4813            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.TypeAliasDeclaration ||                   // type List< |
    4814            8 :                     isFunctionLikeKind(containingNodeKind);
    4815            8 : 
    4816            8 :             case SyntaxKind.StaticKeyword:
    4817            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.PropertyDeclaration && !isClassLike(parent.parent);
    4818            8 : 
    4819            8 :             case SyntaxKind.DotDotDotToken:
    4820            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.Parameter ||
    4821            8 :                     (!!parent.parent && parent.parent.kind === SyntaxKind.ArrayBindingPattern);  // var [...z|
    4822            8 : 
    4823            8 :             case SyntaxKind.PublicKeyword:
    4824            8 :             case SyntaxKind.PrivateKeyword:
    4825            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ProtectedKeyword:
    4826            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.Parameter && !isConstructorDeclaration(parent.parent);
    4827            8 : 
    4828            8 :             case SyntaxKind.AsKeyword:
    4829            8 :                 return containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ImportSpecifier ||
    4830            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ExportSpecifier ||
    4831            8 :                     containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.NamespaceImport;
    4832            8 : 
    4833            8 :             case SyntaxKind.GetKeyword:
    4834            8 :             case SyntaxKind.SetKeyword:
    4835            8 :                 return !isFromObjectTypeDeclaration(contextToken);
    4836            8 : 
    4837            8 :             case SyntaxKind.Identifier: {
    4838            8 :                 if (containingNodeKind === SyntaxKind.ImportSpecifier &&
    4839            8 :                     contextToken === (parent as ImportSpecifier).name &&
    4840            8 :                     (contextToken as Identifier).text === "type"
    4841            8 :                 ) {
    4842            8 :                     // import { type | }
    4843            8 :                     return false;
    4844            8 :                 }

    4846            8 :                     contextToken.parent, isVariableDeclaration);
    4847            8 :                 if (ancestorVariableDeclaration

    4849            8 :                     // let a
    4850            8 :                     // |
    4851            8 :                     return false;
    4852            8 :                 }
    4853            8 :                 break;
    4854            8 :             }
    4855            8 : 
    4856            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ClassKeyword:
    4857            8 :             case SyntaxKind.EnumKeyword:
    4858            8 :             case SyntaxKind.InterfaceKeyword:
    4859            8 :             case SyntaxKind.FunctionKeyword:
    4860            8 :             case SyntaxKind.VarKeyword:
    4861            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ImportKeyword:
    4862            8 :             case SyntaxKind.LetKeyword:
    4863            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ConstKeyword:
    4864            8 :             case SyntaxKind.InferKeyword:
    4865            8 :                 return true;
    4866            8 : 
    4867            8 :             case SyntaxKind.TypeKeyword:
    4868            8 :                 // import { type foo| }
    4869            8 :                 return containingNodeKind !== SyntaxKind.ImportSpecifier;
    4870            8 : 
    4871            8 :             case SyntaxKind.AsteriskToken:
    4872            8 :                 return isFunctionLike(contextToken.parent) && !isMethodDeclaration(contextToken.parent);
    4873            8 :         }
    4874            8 : 
    4875            8 :         // If the previous token is keyword corresponding to class member completion keyword
    4876            8 :         // there will be completion available here
    4877            8 :         if (isClassMemberCompletionKeyword(keywordForNode(contextToken)) && isFromObjectTypeDeclaration(contextToken)) {
    4878            8 :             return false;
    4879            8 :         }
    4880            8 : 
    4881            8 :         if (isConstructorParameterCompletion(contextToken)) {
    4882            8 :             // constructor parameter completion is available only if
    4883            8 :             // - its modifier of the constructor parameter or
    4884            8 :             // - its name of the parameter and not being edited
    4885            8 :             // eg. constructor(a |<- this shouldnt show completion
    4886            8 :             if (
    4887            8 :                 !isIdentifier(contextToken) ||

    4889            8 :                 isCurrentlyEditingNode(contextToken)
    4890            8 :             ) {
    4891            8 :                 return false;
    4892            8 :             }
    4893            8 :         }
    4894            8 : 
    4895            8 :         // Previous token may have been a keyword that was converted to an identifier.
    4896            8 :         switch (keywordForNode(contextToken)) {
    4897            8 :             case SyntaxKind.AbstractKeyword:
    4898            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ClassKeyword:
    4899            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ConstKeyword:
    4900            8 :             case SyntaxKind.DeclareKeyword:
    4901            8 :             case SyntaxKind.EnumKeyword:
    4902            8 :             case SyntaxKind.FunctionKeyword:
    4903            8 :             case SyntaxKind.InterfaceKeyword:
    4904            8 :             case SyntaxKind.LetKeyword:
    4905            8 :             case SyntaxKind.PrivateKeyword:
    4906            8 :             case SyntaxKind.ProtectedKeyword:
    4907            8 :             case SyntaxKind.PublicKeyword:
    4908            8 :             case SyntaxKind.StaticKeyword:
    4909            8 :             case SyntaxKind.VarKeyword:
    4910            8 :                 return true;
    4911            8 :             case SyntaxKind.AsyncKeyword:
    4912            8 :                 return isPropertyDeclaration(contextToken.parent);
    4913            8 :         }
    4914            8 : 
    4915            8 :         // If we are inside a class declaration, and `constructor` is totally not present,
    4916            8 :         // but we request a completion manually at a whitespace...
    4917            8 :         const ancestorClassLike = findAncestor(contextToken.parent, isClassLike);
    4918            8 :         if (ancestorClassLike && contextToken === previousToken && isPreviousPropertyDeclarationTerminated(contextToken, position)) {
    4919            8 :             return false; // Don't block completions.
    4920            8 :         }
    4921            8 : 
    4922            8 :         const ancestorPropertyDeclaraion = getAncestor(contextToken.parent, SyntaxKind.PropertyDeclaration);
    4923            8 :         // If we are inside a class declaration and typing `constructor` after property declaration...
    4924            8 :         if (
    4925            8 :             ancestorPropertyDeclaraion
    4926            8 :             && contextToken !== previousToken
    4927            8 :             && isClassLike(previousToken.parent.parent)
    4928            8 :             // And the cursor is at the token...
    4929            8 :             && position <= previousToken.end
    4930            8 :         ) {
    4931            8 :             // If we are sure that the previous property declaration is terminated according to newline or semicolon...
    4932            8 :             if (isPreviousPropertyDeclarationTerminated(contextToken, previousToken.end)) {
    4933            8 :                 return false; // Don't block completions.
    4934            8 :             }
    4935            8 :             else if (
    4936            8 :                 contextToken.kind !== SyntaxKind.EqualsToken
    4937            8 :                 // Should not block: `class C { blah = c/**/ }`
    4938            8 :                 // But should block: `class C { blah = somewhat c/**/ }` and `class C { blah: SomeType c/**/ }`
    4939            8 :                 && (isInitializedProperty(ancestorPropertyDeclaraion as PropertyDeclaration)
    4940            8 :                     || hasType(ancestorPropertyDeclaraion))

    4942            8 :                 return true;
    4943            8 :             }
    4944            8 :         }
    4945            8 : 
    4946            8 :         return isDeclarationName(contextToken)
    4947            8 :             && !isShorthandPropertyAssignment(contextToken.parent)
    4948            8 :             && !isJsxAttribute(contextToken.parent)
    4949            8 :             // Don't block completions if we're in `class C /**/`, `interface I /**/` or `<T /**/>` , because we're *past* the end of the identifier and might want to complete `extends`.
    4950            8 :             // If `contextToken !== previousToken`, this is `class C ex/**/`, `interface I ex/**/` or `<T ex/**/>`.
    4951            8 :             && !((isClassLike(contextToken.parent) || isInterfaceDeclaration(contextToken.parent) || isTypeParameterDeclaration(contextToken.parent)) && (contextToken !== previousToken || position > previousToken.end));
    4952            8 :     }
    4953            8 : 
    4954            8 :     function isPreviousPropertyDeclarationTerminated(contextToken: Node, position: number) {
    4955            8 :         return contextToken.kind !== SyntaxKind.EqualsToken &&
    4956            8 :             (contextToken.kind === SyntaxKind.SemicolonToken
    4957            8 :                 || !positionsAreOnSameLine(contextToken.end, position, sourceFile));
    4958            8 :     }

    4978            8 :     /**
    4979            8 :      * Filters out completion suggestions for named imports or exports.
    4980            8 :      *
    4981            8 :      * @returns Symbols to be suggested in an object binding pattern or object literal expression, barring those whose declarations
    4982            8 :      *          do not occur at the current position and have not otherwise been typed.
    4983            8 :      */
    4984            8 :     function filterObjectMembersList(contextualMemberSymbols: Symbol[], existingMembers: readonly Declaration[]): Symbol[] {
    4985            8 :         if (existingMembers.length === 0) {
    4986            8 :             return contextualMemberSymbols;
    4987            8 :         }
    4988            8 : 
    4989            8 :         const membersDeclaredBySpreadAssignment = new Set<string>();
    4990            8 :         const existingMemberNames = new Set<__String>();
    4991            8 :         for (const m of existingMembers) {
    4992            8 :             // Ignore omitted expressions for missing members
    4993            8 :             if (
    4994            8 :                 m.kind !== SyntaxKind.PropertyAssignment &&
    4995            8 :                 m.kind !== SyntaxKind.ShorthandPropertyAssignment &&
    4996            8 :                 m.kind !== SyntaxKind.BindingElement &&

    5003            8 :             }

    5018            8 :                     existingName = m.propertyName.escapedText;
    5019            8 :                 }
    5020            8 :             }

    5036            8 :

    5040            8 :     function setMembersDeclaredBySpreadAssignment(declaration: SpreadAssignment | JsxSpreadAttribute, membersDeclaredBySpreadAssignment: Set<string>) {

    5042            8 :         const symbol = typeChecker.getSymbolAtLocation(expression);
    5043            8 :         const type = symbol && typeChecker.getTypeOfSymbolAtLocation(symbol, expression);
    5044            8 :         const properties = type && (type as ObjectType).properties;
    5045            8 :         if (properties) {
    5046            8 :             properties.forEach(property => {
    5047            8 :                 membersDeclaredBySpreadAssignment.add(property.name);
    5048            8 :             });
    5049            8 :         }
    5050            8 :     }

    5052            8 :     // Set SortText to OptionalMember if it is an optional member
    5053            8 :     function setSortTextToOptionalMember() {
    5054            8 :         symbols.forEach(m => {
    5055            8 :             if (m.flags & SymbolFlags.Optional) {
    5056            8 :                 const symbolId = getSymbolId(m);
    5057            8 :                 symbolToSortTextMap[symbolId] = symbolToSortTextMap[symbolId] ?? SortText.OptionalMember;
    5058            8 :             }
    5059            8 :         });
    5060            8 :     }

    5062            8 :     // Set SortText to MemberDeclaredBySpreadAssignment if it is fulfilled by spread assignment
    5063            8 :     function setSortTextToMemberDeclaredBySpreadAssignment(membersDeclaredBySpreadAssignment: Set<string>, contextualMemberSymbols: Symbol[]): void {
    5064            8 :         if (membersDeclaredBySpreadAssignment.size === 0) {
    5065            8 :             return;
    5066            8 :         }
    5067            8 :         for (const contextualMemberSymbol of contextualMemberSymbols) {
    5068            8 :             if (membersDeclaredBySpreadAssignment.has(contextualMemberSymbol.name)) {
    5069            8 :                 symbolToSortTextMap[getSymbolId(contextualMemberSymbol)] = SortText.MemberDeclaredBySpreadAssignment;
    5070            8 :             }
    5071            8 :         }
    5072            8 :     }

    5074            8 :     function transformObjectLiteralMembersSortText(start: number): void {
    5075            8 :         for (let i = start; i < symbols.length; i++) {
    5076            8 :             const symbol = symbols[i];
    5077            8 :             const symbolId = getSymbolId(symbol);
    5078            8 :             const origin = symbolToOriginInfoMap?.[i];
    5079            8 :             const target = getEmitScriptTarget(compilerOptions);
    5080            8 :             const displayName = getCompletionEntryDisplayNameForSymbol(
    5081            8 :                 symbol,
    5082            8 :                 target,
    5083            8 :                 origin,
    5084            8 :                 CompletionKind.ObjectPropertyDeclaration,
    5085            8 :                 /*jsxIdentifierExpected*/ false,
    5086            8 :             );
    5087            8 :             if (displayName) {
    5088            8 :                 const originalSortText = symbolToSortTextMap[symbolId] ?? SortText.LocationPriority;
    5089            8 :                 const { name } = displayName;
    5090            8 :                 symbolToSortTextMap[symbolId] = SortText.ObjectLiteralProperty(originalSortText, name);
    5091            8 :             }
    5092            8 :         }
    5093            8 :     }

    5095            8 :     /**
